<h1>P&Ecirc;ŞGOTIN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi nav&ecirc; Xweday&ecirc; mezin</p>
<p>B&icirc;sm&icirc;llah em destp&ecirc; dikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bib&ecirc;jin pesn &ucirc; selat</p>
<p>Paş&ecirc; em bikin xebat</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezar nehsed heft&ecirc; sis&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;n ez hatime din&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rastiy&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; dizane</p>
<p>Ev gor nasnama Tirkane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mezin&ecirc; me t&ecirc;n ji Motkan</p>
<p>Ji wir di&ccedil;in Gely&ecirc; Z&icirc;lan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Paş&ecirc; t&ecirc;ne Xirabşer&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bic&icirc;dibin li v&ecirc; der&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Malbata me Mexsoy&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Ji eş&icirc;reta Motk&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bav&ecirc; min Salh&ecirc; M&icirc;rze ye</p>
<p>Dayika min Zubeyde ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şeş zarok Xwed&ecirc; dane me</p>
<p>Yek stand p&ecirc;nc man li cem me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min li ser van şeş zarokan</p>
<p>Helbest &ccedil;&ecirc;kir bi nav&ecirc; wan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku h&ucirc;n pirt&ucirc;k&ecirc; bixw&icirc;nin</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n&ecirc; di nav da bib&icirc;nin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi pirran&icirc; helbest&ecirc;n min</p>
<p>Qetek ji jiyana min in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hinek jiyan hinek h&ecirc;v&icirc;</p>
<p>Min kom kirin n&ecirc;v&icirc; n&ecirc;v&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav dan&icirc; Hebana Berxvan</p>
<p>Gir&ecirc;da li pişta xortan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bona ber tav&ecirc; hişk nebin</p>
<p>Derfeta xwarina wan hebin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Keremkin ser sifra Berxvan</p>
<p>Ne&ecirc;şin bibe loş&icirc;can</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bibexş&icirc;nin k&ecirc;masiyan</p>
<p>Gazin nekin ji gundiyan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;mkan&ecirc; wan z&ecirc;de n&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Xweştir dikin biqed&icirc;nin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tal &ucirc; t&ucirc;j &ucirc; tirş ji me ra</p>
<p>Şir&icirc;n afyet be ji we ra</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>P&Ecirc;XEMBER&Ecirc; ME (s.)</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Selamullah li te be</p>
<p>Tu qasid&ecirc; Xweda y&icirc;</p>
<p>J&rsquo;me ra şefa&rsquo;et bike</p>
<p>Tu roniya &ccedil;ava y&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu qasid&ecirc; Xweda y&icirc;</p>
<p>Tu roniya &ccedil;ava y&icirc;</p>
<p>Destgir&ecirc; feq&icirc;ra y&icirc;</p>
<p>Tu derman&ecirc; derda y&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;Ebdullah bav&ecirc; te ye</p>
<p>Dayka te Am&icirc;ne ye</p>
<p>Bajar&ecirc; te Mekke ye</p>
<p>Tirba te l&rsquo;Med&icirc;ne ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;&lsquo;Umr&ecirc; te ş&ecirc;sts&ecirc; sal e</p>
<p>Te jvir kir &icirc;rt&icirc;hal e</p>
<p>Ji dost ra kir w&icirc;sal e</p>
<p>Te behişt kire male</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Du ş&ecirc;r neviy&ecirc; te ne</p>
<p>Hesen Huseyn bi xwe ne</p>
<p>Delaly&ecirc; Fat&icirc;me ne</p>
<p>R&ecirc;zan&ecirc; r&ecirc;ya me ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zavay&ecirc; te &lsquo;El&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Fatima bi x&ecirc;l&icirc; ye</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo &lsquo;Eliy&ecirc; wel&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Dibim ax &ucirc; xwel&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zavay&ecirc; din &lsquo;Usman e</p>
<p>Ew şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; Qur&rsquo;an e</p>
<p>Ew xwedy&ecirc; du n&ucirc;ra ne</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo w&icirc; dibim qurbane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dinya j&rsquo;bo te b&ucirc; ava</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo hem&icirc; d&ecirc;y&ucirc; bava</p>
<p>Pez &ccedil;&ucirc;ne l&rsquo;ser delava</p>
<p>Me d&icirc;t ev nan &ucirc; ava</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez ji dil &ucirc; hinava</p>
<p>Li te dikim silava</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo &Icirc;slam bibe ava</p>
<p>Ji Xweda dikim lava</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;slam d&icirc;nek p&icirc;roz e</p>
<p>B&icirc;na xweş dide poze</p>
<p>J&rsquo;me ra wek&icirc; newroz e</p>
<p>Xweda tu bike doze</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew dozeke ez&icirc;z e</p>
<p>Pir delale tem&icirc;z e</p>
<p>Bi te&rsquo;m e pir lez&icirc;z e</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo bav, law, d&ecirc;y &ucirc; q&icirc;z e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bo p&icirc;r ji bo kala</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo feq&icirc;r j&rsquo;bo bi mala</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo dosta j&rsquo;bo hevala</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo rasta j&rsquo;bo delala</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo mirya ji bo cana</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo gund &ucirc; mal &ucirc; xana</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo m&icirc;ra j&rsquo;bo şivana</p>
<p>Ji bo hem&icirc; &icirc;nsana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo dinya &ucirc; axret&ecirc;</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo xal, ap, xalt&icirc;, met&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ji bo ehl&ecirc; x&icirc;ret&ecirc;</p>
<p>J&rsquo;bo kes&ecirc;n li ser xet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>T&ecirc;ra dinyay&ecirc; heye</p>
<p>Ji her doz&icirc; z&ecirc;de ye</p>
<p>Xweda şand ji bo me ye</p>
<p>Ew heqe ol&ecirc; me ye.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>MIZG&Icirc;N&Icirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>L&rsquo;ser dinyay&ecirc; bib&ucirc; zulmet</p>
<p>Dilan da nemab&ucirc; şifqet</p>
<p>Derket N&ucirc;ra H&icirc;dayet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Aleman ra an&icirc; rihmet</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Alem ketib&ucirc;n nav ş&icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>Q&icirc;r&icirc;n b&ucirc; her der&ecirc;n din&ecirc;</p>
<p>M&ucirc;hemmed Eleyh&icirc;s-selam</p>
<p>Ji me ra an&icirc; mizg&icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zarok jin tev dinaliyan</p>
<p>Gir&icirc;n b&ucirc; hem&icirc; aliyan</p>
<p>Derket Xatemul Enbiya</p>
<p>Derman kir derd&ecirc; s&ecirc;wiyan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&ecirc; bi h&ecirc;z be ew xwed&icirc; heq</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc;n b&ecirc;kes hero niheq</p>
<p>Hat dadmendiya &Icirc;slam&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li ser zilm&ecirc; kir teqe teq</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Batil di&ccedil;e ku heq were</p>
<p>Diqede derd &ucirc; kedere</p>
<p>Xelaskar&ecirc; herdu alem</p>
<p>M&ucirc;hemmed j&rsquo;me ra r&ecirc;ber e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hewar dikir hem&icirc; m&icirc;llet</p>
<p>Hal&ecirc; wana bib&ucirc; z&icirc;llet</p>
<p>Rahmeten l&icirc;l alem&icirc;n hat</p>
<p>Merivan ra an&icirc; &icirc;zzet</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi nav&ecirc; şir&icirc;n M&ucirc;hemmed</p>
<p>Di &Icirc;nc&icirc;l&ecirc; da ew Ahmed</p>
<p>Tu roniya &ccedil;av&ecirc; me y&icirc;</p>
<p>Qasid&ecirc; Xweday&ecirc; Semed</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gerd&ucirc;n&ecirc; da tine wefa</p>
<p>&Icirc;mt&icirc;han nabe b&ecirc; cefa</p>
<p>Bajo doza Heb&icirc;b&ucirc;llah</p>
<p>Bo şefa&rsquo;et ke Mustefa</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mizg&icirc;n dide Res&ucirc;l&ucirc;llah</p>
<p>Ku h&ucirc;n rast bibin &lsquo;Ebdullah</p>
<p>Ji dojeh&ecirc; we d&ucirc;r dike</p>
<p>Diş&icirc;ne buhişt&ecirc; Ellah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Qul la &icirc;lahe &icirc;llallah</p>
<p>Heq M&ucirc;hemmed Res&ucirc;lullah</p>
<p>Wexf&icirc;rlena zun&ucirc;bena</p>
<p>Werhemna ya Reh&icirc;mellah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>AM&Icirc;N</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez &lsquo;evdek&icirc; gunehkar im</p>
<p>Jar &ucirc; feq&icirc;r ist&ucirc;xwar im</p>
<p>JRebb&ecirc; Xef&ucirc;r h&ecirc;v&icirc;dar im</p>
<p>Ya Reb tu h&ecirc;vy&ecirc; biş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Am&icirc;n am&icirc;n am&icirc;n Am&icirc;n</p>

<h1>ROJEKE ZIVISTAN&Ecirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Nav merzel bi tevir b&ecirc;r in</p>

<p>Wefat kirye p&icirc;rka Melek</p>

<p>Tevd&icirc;ra gor&ecirc; b&icirc;r nekin</p>

<h1>KEK SEYDA &Icirc;ZZEDD&Icirc;N</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; bi diyar&ecirc; Eyubsultan&ecirc; li şewitya Stembol&ecirc; diketim &icirc;ro li min sar e</p>
<p>Kula Xwed&ecirc; bi kul be bikeve nava fesad &ucirc; xay&icirc;na kes&ecirc; ji Seyday&ecirc; min ra b&ucirc;ne b&ecirc;bext &ucirc; neyare</p>
<p>Ji Kek&ecirc; min&ecirc; Şeh&icirc;d Seyday&ecirc; h&ecirc;ja Mele &Icirc;zzedd&icirc;n ra b&ucirc;ne gur&ecirc; hare</p>
<p>Ez &ccedil;i bikim &ccedil;i nekim min heyfa seyday&ecirc; xwe hilneda mel&ucirc;l im pir b&ecirc; hal im dinalim ez mame &lsquo;evdal &ucirc; b&ecirc;&ccedil;are</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li we be. Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n Seyday&ecirc; min serok&ecirc; min eg&icirc;t&ecirc; min şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; min delal&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li Umrany&ecirc; ciy&ecirc; Seyday&ecirc; xwe dinh&ecirc;rim bilinde biny&ecirc; dar e</p>
<p>Şakird mane b&ecirc; Seyda qonaxa delal&ecirc; min valaye ist&ucirc;xwar e</p>
<p>Kesek tine cavek&ecirc; bibe Panos&ecirc; Qerekos&ecirc; na welle Kurdistan&ecirc; li c&icirc;han&ecirc; ji Kurd&ecirc; bawermend&ecirc; m&ecirc;rxas &ucirc; eg&icirc;t bixwaze heware</p>
<p>Belk&icirc; seyda mezin &ucirc; rewşenb&icirc;r &ucirc; gire gir&ecirc; kalem&ecirc;r tev&ecirc; ciwan &ucirc; xort&ecirc;n delal werin li doza seyday&ecirc; min bipirsin, ku nepirsin mirin ji bo me teva ye, dinya mal&ecirc; kes&icirc; n&icirc;ne, ji kes&icirc; ra nabe milk &ucirc; ware.</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li we be. Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n Seyday&ecirc; min serok&ecirc; min eg&icirc;t&ecirc; min şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; min delal&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li k&ecirc;leka gol&ecirc; li kevir&ecirc; Kela Wan&ecirc; dinh&ecirc;rim dil&ecirc; min dike zare zare</p>
<p>Ku h&ucirc;n b&ecirc;jin: Doza Seyday&ecirc; te &ccedil;iye? Ez&ecirc; b&ecirc;jim Gula Zehra ye wesyeta Ustad e, Seyday&ecirc; min ji bon&ecirc; dixebit&icirc; dikir kare</p>
<p>Kevir&ecirc; Kela Wan&ecirc; k&ecirc;lik&ecirc; Bed&icirc;uzzeman e, Kurdistan merqeda w&icirc; ye, em wesyeta w&icirc; bi c&icirc; b&icirc;nin, gulek&ecirc; bi&ccedil;ik&icirc;nin li v&icirc; welat&icirc; li v&icirc; ware</p>
<p>Bila zarok&ecirc; Kurda herin Medresa Zehra, bixw&icirc;nin p&ecirc;şda herin ders&ecirc; bidin dinyay&ecirc;, şad&ucirc; h&ecirc;say&ucirc; k&ecirc;fxweş bikin dil&ecirc; dost &ucirc; yare, bila kul bikin dil&ecirc; dijmin, dil&ecirc; b&ecirc;bext&ecirc; neyar e.</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li we be. Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n Seyday&ecirc; min serok&ecirc; min &lsquo;eg&icirc;t&ecirc; min şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; min delal&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li &ccedil;erxa felek&ecirc; li hal&ecirc; dinyalik&ecirc; dinh&ecirc;rim nal&icirc;n &ucirc; zarezar e</p>
<p>Zalim pir in maf&ecirc; feq&icirc;ra, b&ecirc;kesa dixwin wan dih&ecirc;lin b&ecirc;pare</p>
<p>Xweda kes&ecirc; b&ecirc;kesane &ccedil;ara b&ecirc;&ccedil;arane del&icirc;l&ecirc; muteheyy&icirc;rane Qadir&ecirc; Zulcelale ji me ra dost &ucirc; yare</p>
<p>Hey zalimno hey kujerno hey teresno hey b&ecirc;bextno h&ucirc;n bizanin bilerizin dinya bi dor e ne bi zor e ew zilm&ucirc; zordariya ku h&ucirc;n dikin w&ecirc; b&ecirc;fil&ecirc; we ra were xar&ecirc; ji we ra nam&icirc;ne kare.</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li we be. Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n Seyday&ecirc; min serok&ecirc; min eg&icirc;t&ecirc; min şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; min delal&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; min.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li Deşta Milazgir&ecirc; rasta Panos&ecirc; Gund&ecirc; Qizilqay&ecirc;, Qerehesen&ecirc; diketim hav&icirc;ne wa hav&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Ces&icirc;m dib&ecirc; Huseyn&ecirc; bira malik neşewityo de rabe, ser&ecirc; xwe rake, &ccedil;ava veke ji v&ecirc; xewa şir&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Pişt&icirc; şeh&icirc;db&ucirc;na Seyday&ecirc; Mele &Icirc;zzed&icirc;n li w&ecirc;rana Antalya wefat kirye Seyfedd&icirc;n&ecirc; N&ucirc;jdar&ecirc; heval&ecirc; Seyda ew xizmeta wane giranbiha ma h&ecirc;viya me &lsquo;evdala derd&ecirc; min girane hal&ecirc; min tin&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ca tu rabe here cav&ecirc; bide Ra&icirc;f&ecirc; B&ecirc;&ccedil;are bav&ecirc; &Icirc;hsan N&ucirc;r&icirc; xelq&ecirc; Gely&ecirc; Z&icirc;lan bila kilamek&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;ke bilor&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bila m&ecirc;r&ecirc; tofan &ucirc; teşqela &lsquo;Evdilah&ecirc; &ccedil;avbelek tev&ecirc; eg&icirc;t&ecirc; xorta, ş&ecirc;x &ucirc; meşayixa, mezin &ucirc; r&ecirc;zana p&ecirc; bihes&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Belk&icirc; xwe bihej&icirc;nin xebata xwe z&ecirc;dekin ev xizmeta Qurana P&icirc;roz d&icirc;n&ecirc; mub&icirc;n zel&icirc;l nebe li erd&ecirc; nem&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li we be. Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n Seyday&ecirc; min serok&ecirc; min eg&icirc;t&ecirc; min şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; min delal&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; min.</p>

<h1>HEZKIRIN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezkirin hebe di dila</p>
<p>Meriv dibe m&icirc;na gula</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Riy&ecirc; meriv p&ecirc; dibe geş</p>
<p>K&ecirc; bib&icirc;ne dibe k&ecirc;fxweş</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew meriv&ecirc; k&ecirc;fxweş r&ucirc;şen</p>
<p>Meriv bi w&icirc; dibe r&ucirc;ken</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ewan kes&ecirc;n sik&ucirc;mmoloz</p>
<p>Xeber didin bi ser&ecirc; poz</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Meriv&ecirc; wana bib&icirc;ne</p>
<p>B&icirc;z&ecirc; xwe ji wana t&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ecirc;var bi wan nabe sibe</p>
<p>Meriv ji wan aciz dibe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezkirina ji bo Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>B&ecirc; hember&icirc; m&icirc;na ya d&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kezeva dayka dipije</p>
<p>Bo zar&ecirc; xwe, xwe dikuje</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Canf&icirc;day&ecirc; hezkirin&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nizanin nefret &ucirc; k&icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezkirin Xweda da me ye</p>
<p>T&ecirc;ra &lsquo;alem&ecirc; tev heye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku em timatiy&ecirc; nekin</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; hezkirn&ecirc; z&ecirc;de kin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ser&icirc; da hezkin ji Ellah</p>
<p>D&ucirc; w&icirc; ra ji Heb&icirc;b&ucirc;llah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Paş&ecirc; hem&icirc; p&ecirc;xemberan</p>
<p>D&ucirc;ra zana &ucirc; r&ecirc;beran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezke ji qenca, delala</p>
<p>Ji biraya ji hevala</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezke ji d&ecirc; bav &ucirc; kala</p>
<p>Ji ap &ucirc; met, xat&icirc;, xala</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Malx&ecirc; hezke ji bermaly&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kar giran be, here aly&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bermal&icirc; hezke ji malx&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ay&ecirc; bibe ber p&ucirc;lix&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji zara hezkin bi şifqet</p>
<p>Xweda li we bike rihmet</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezkin ji feq&icirc;r &ucirc; jara</p>
<p>Li wana nexin bi dara</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji b&ecirc;kesa ji r&ecirc;wiya</p>
<p>Ji &ecirc;t&icirc;ma ji s&ecirc;wiya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji seqeta ji bir&ccedil;iya</p>
<p>Ji b&ecirc;&ccedil;areya ji tiya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bajarya ji gundiya</p>
<p>Ji jineb&icirc; m&ecirc;rebiya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezkirna dila b&ecirc;hede</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iqas hezk&icirc; ew naqede.</p>

<h1>P&Icirc;ROZNAME</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Doza we doz dikim</p>
<p>Xwel ber we xoz dikim</p>
<p>Roja eş&ucirc;r&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li we p&icirc;roz dikim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Selam diş&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Husey&icirc;n b&icirc;r t&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Ji bo r&ucirc;h&ecirc; wan</p>
<p>Quran dixw&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Eş&ucirc;re p&icirc;roz be</p>
<p>Hingiv&ecirc; moz be</p>
<p>&Icirc;nşallah v&ecirc; doz&ecirc;</p>
<p>D&ecirc; bajom soz be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>Ş&Ecirc;X&Ecirc; MIN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li Wartoy&ecirc; li Gimgim&ecirc; dinh&ecirc;rim dil&ecirc; min dizare.</p>
<p>Kal&ecirc; Ş&ecirc;x Se&icirc;d li vir girtye b&ecirc;bext&ecirc; neyar e.</p>
<p>Kal&ecirc; min tev&ecirc; gelek eg&icirc;ta şeh&icirc;dkirin, birin &icirc;dam&ecirc; dardakirin li dar e.</p>
<p>Ew &ccedil;&ucirc;ne dinya heq, heyfa wan ma li erd&ecirc;, kes tine ez digr&icirc;m ji Xana Kerem&ecirc; Xaliq M&icirc;r&ecirc; M&icirc;ra dixwazim heware.</p>
<p>Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n, Ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; min, P&icirc;r&ecirc; min, Sultan&ecirc; min, M&icirc;r&ecirc; min.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zivistan e, serma ye, r&ucirc;y&ecirc; erd&ecirc; li me sar e.</p>
<p>Kula Xwed&ecirc; bikeve nava xay&icirc;n&ecirc; neyare.</p>
<p>Xweday&ecirc; Mezin nevy&ecirc; Ş&ecirc;x Se&icirc;d hişyar bike, li doza Ş&ecirc;x&ecirc;m bike yare.</p>
<p>Bila tola şeh&icirc;da hildin li cem Xwed&ecirc; ji me ra b&icirc;nin hewar &ucirc; sitar e.</p>
<p>Em layiq&ecirc; we neb&ucirc;n, Ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; min, P&icirc;r&ecirc; min, Sultan&ecirc; min, M&icirc;r&ecirc; min.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>MEKTEB</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwendin ji bo p&ecirc;şve&ccedil;&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>Ne ji bona zilm&ucirc; x&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>&Icirc;ro tij&icirc; teres b&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>Bese bira ji xew rabe</p>
<p>B&ecirc;je xwendin awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Neyar&ecirc; nezan&ecirc; &lsquo;ilm e</p>
<p>Li dev&ecirc; w&ecirc; dixe kulme</p>
<p>&lsquo;Ilim were di&ccedil;e zilme</p>
<p>Li ber nezaniy&ecirc; rabe</p>
<p>B&ecirc;je mekteb awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Agir,bar&ucirc;t an&icirc;n ber hev</p>
<p>Xinz&icirc;rtiye bi roj &ucirc; şev</p>
<p>Nam&ucirc;s&ecirc; ra pir şerm e ev</p>
<p>Gelo hal&ecirc; me y&ecirc; &ccedil;a be</p>
<p>B&ecirc;je x&icirc;ret awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>X&icirc;ret nam&ucirc;s dike hewar</p>
<p>Pirr&ecirc;n &icirc;nsan b&ucirc;ne xewar</p>
<p>Qet şerm nakin b&ucirc;ne dewar</p>
<p>Bira &ecirc;d&icirc; ji xew rabe</p>
<p>&Icirc;nsanet&icirc; awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di sifet&ecirc; &icirc;nsanan da</p>
<p>Pir b&ucirc;ne heywan&ecirc;n Xweda</p>
<p>Wan der&ecirc; xwendin&ecirc; dada</p>
<p>Bira bese ji xew rabe</p>
<p>Mislimant&icirc; awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev mekteb tella deccal e</p>
<p>Em ketin&ecirc; heşt&ecirc; sale</p>
<p>Me jib&icirc;rkir bav &ucirc; kale</p>
<p>Li ber deccal&icirc;zm&ecirc; rabe</p>
<p>Ev kolet&icirc; awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji Xwed&ecirc; ra spas bike</p>
<p>Belk&icirc; ew me xelas bike</p>
<p>Dinyay&ecirc; da &ccedil;av nas bike</p>
<p>Bira b&ecirc;je Allah rabe</p>
<p>Ev teral&icirc; awha nabe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>WERE &Icirc;MAN&Ecirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;slam &ccedil;iqas şir&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Were tu j&icirc; bib&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Zehmet&ecirc; da nem&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Xelas be biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xweda tu afirand&icirc;</p>
<p>Bo &lsquo;evd&icirc;tiy&ecirc; şand&icirc;</p>
<p>Ecel were t&ecirc; cand&icirc;</p>
<p>Bizanibe biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>P&ecirc;xember&ecirc; omet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bo bike şefa&rsquo;et&ecirc;</p>
<p>Hinek bike xebat&ecirc;</p>
<p>X&icirc;retke biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Sed hezar p&ecirc;xemberan</p>
<p>Wel&icirc; şeh&icirc;d r&ecirc;beran</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;jin heq xeberan</p>
<p>Bawerke biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bed&icirc;uzzeman Xan&icirc;</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;jin dinya fan&icirc;</p>
<p>Xwe m&ecirc;zeke tu &ccedil;an&icirc;</p>
<p>Nexape biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; xwe vek&icirc; bigr&icirc;</p>
<p>Hew nih&ecirc;r&icirc; tu mir&icirc;</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; herin axir&icirc;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;van&icirc; biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dijmin te nexap&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Mal &ucirc; can&ecirc; xwe b&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Tu buhişt&ecirc; bist&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ji Xweda biray&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira were &icirc;man&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bira were Quran&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bira were &Icirc;slam&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xelas be biray&ecirc; min</p>

<h1>MEDRESA ZEHRA</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bihar&ecirc; were ku &ccedil;&ucirc; zivistan</p>
<p>Gulek&ecirc; vebe li nav Kurdistan</p>
<p>Mizg&icirc;niy&ecirc; bide hem&icirc; &icirc;nsan</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li wan&ecirc; vebe Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Medresa Ezher ji te ra bira</p>
<p>Dest&ecirc; hev bigrin h&ucirc;n bibin &ccedil;ira</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ar aliy&ecirc; te mum&icirc;n &lsquo;evd&icirc;stan</p>
<p>Ereb &ucirc; Faris &Ccedil;erkez Tirk&icirc;stan</p>
<p>Tev bibin bira Laz &ucirc; Kurdistan</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Wacib e t&ecirc; da ziman&ecirc; Ereb</p>
<p>Lazime ziman&ecirc; Tirk&icirc; j&icirc; heb</p>
<p>Kurd&icirc; ca&icirc;ze b&ecirc; şerm &ucirc; b&ecirc; eyb</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;Ilm&ecirc; d&icirc;n &ucirc; fen hev hem&ecirc;z dikin</p>
<p>Misliman hem&icirc; ji hev hez dikin</p>
<p>&Icirc;tt&icirc;hada &Icirc;slam&ecirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;dikin</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Se&icirc;d&ecirc; Kurd&icirc; j&rsquo;te ra xebit&icirc;</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; w&icirc; b&ecirc; hed li me şewit&icirc;</p>
<p>Ji omet&ecirc; ra tu lazim d&icirc;t&icirc;</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dijmin&ecirc; me s&ecirc; ne yek nezan&icirc;</p>
<p>Yek &icirc;xt&icirc;laf ya din j&icirc; xizan&icirc;</p>
<p>Ş&ucirc;r in yek&icirc;t&icirc; huner &ucirc; zan&icirc;</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r hat&icirc; tu Medresa Zehra</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; misliman rast bibin bira</p>

<h1>&Ccedil;END HEVAL</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; were em herin</p>
<p>Em du teyr&ecirc; b&ecirc; per in</p>
<p>Li van dera digerin</p>
<p>Nefsa xwe ra bi şer in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;ro ji roja &icirc;ne</p>
<p>Eyd e l&ecirc; betlan n&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&lsquo;Ewr &ucirc; ezman bi ş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Nefis kore nab&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ecirc;ja ye Kek&ecirc; Aydin</p>
<p>R&icirc;sale kirye d&ucirc;rb&icirc;n</p>
<p>Dixwaze ku werger&icirc;n</p>
<p>Bi zimanek&icirc; şir&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ayhan ji Meretowar</p>
<p>Li ser Kurd&icirc; dike kar</p>

<h1>B&Ecirc;HEMD&Icirc;T&Icirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ecirc;hemd&icirc;t&icirc; ji &ccedil;iye</p>
<p>Min li ser xwe d&icirc;tiye</p>
<p>Ne carek ne b&icirc;st s&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Ku ez b&ecirc; hemd&ecirc; xwe me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Haya min ji min tuneye</p>
<p>Li dinyay&ecirc; &ccedil;i heye</p>
<p>Ne yek ne sed hevde ye</p>
<p>Ku ez b&ecirc; hemd&ecirc; xwe me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ber bi gorr&ecirc; dimeşim</p>
<p>B&ecirc; aqil &ucirc; b&ecirc; hişim</p>
<p>Ne &ccedil;er&ccedil;&icirc; ne dewr&ecirc;ş im</p>
<p>Ku ez b&ecirc; hemd&ecirc; xwe me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Guneha ez d&icirc;n kirim</p>
<p>Weke hesp&ecirc; z&icirc;n kirim</p>
<p>Ne giryam ne ş&icirc;n kirim</p>
<p>Ku ez b&ecirc;hemd&ecirc; xwe me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gur girt&icirc;me weke pez</p>
<p>Azad&icirc; ra nakim lez</p>
<p>Ne sadiq&ecirc; doz&ecirc; ez</p>
<p>Ku ez b&ecirc; hemd&ecirc; xwe me</p>

<h1>ŞABIN BIRA</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zagon&ecirc; &lsquo;evda tev ceribandin</p>
<p>Derd&ecirc; kes&icirc; qet sivik nekirin</p>
<p>H&ecirc; derd z&ecirc;dekir &lsquo;evd belengaz kir</p>
<p>Em wan naxwazin em&ecirc; wan rakin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tar&icirc;tiya zilm&ecirc; winda dibe</p>
<p>N&ucirc;ra &icirc;man&ecirc; pir şemal dide</p>
<p>Pişta zalima zordesta dişk&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ku deng&ecirc; &Icirc;slam&ecirc; bilind dibe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;zim&ecirc; du r&ucirc; tev &icirc;flas dikin</p>
<p>Hindik maye ku ew bixeniqin</p>
<p>Sanciy&ecirc;, &ecirc;ş&ecirc; bi wan girtiye</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima mucah&icirc;d ku xebat dikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bed&icirc;uzzeman, Ş&ecirc;x Se&icirc;d hatin</p>
<p>P&icirc;c&ecirc; &ccedil;av h&ecirc;ş&icirc;n h&ucirc;n bilerizin</p>
<p>Selahedd&icirc;n&ecirc; ser&ecirc; we j&ecirc;kin</p>
<p>Leşker&ecirc; bixa&ccedil; h&ucirc;n ku da di&ccedil;in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku &Icirc;slam were derd&ecirc; hindik bin</p>
<p>Keser &ucirc; kul &ucirc; keder sivik bin</p>
<p>Ezab&ecirc; li ser w&icirc;cdanan rabe</p>
<p>He&ccedil;iy&ecirc; mezl&ucirc;m w&ecirc; k&ecirc;fxweş bibin</p>

<h1>K&Icirc;JAN H&Ecirc;JA YE</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di v&ecirc; m&ecirc;vanxan&ecirc; de</p>
<p>Her şuxl&ecirc; ku em t&ecirc; de</p>
<p>Em didin ber &ccedil;av&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>Bi zirar &ucirc; bi f&ecirc;de</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tişt&ecirc;n zirar em nakin</p>
<p>Em dixwazin wan rakin</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc;n b&ecirc; berjewend&icirc;</p>
<p>Ka em&ecirc; wana &ccedil;akin!</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bona em bikin kar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Div&ecirc;t fehmkin zirar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bo hev veqetana wan</p>
<p>Hessas bin wek radar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi m&ecirc;z&icirc;n&ecirc; bikş&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Al&ecirc; giran hil&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc; sivik bav&ecirc;jin</p>
<p>Paş&ecirc; x&ecirc;r&ecirc; bib&icirc;nin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&ecirc; ku xwe nexap&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Mal &ucirc; ruh&ecirc; xwe b&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ji w&icirc; Xweday&ecirc; Semed</p>
<p>W&ecirc; bih&icirc;şt&ecirc; bist&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gir&icirc;ng e &ccedil;i m&ecirc;z&icirc;n e?</p>
<p>Ew Qurana mub&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Tişta rind n&icirc;şan dide</p>
<p>Ew rasttirin d&ucirc;rb&icirc;n e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hiş&ecirc; beşera k&ecirc;m e</p>
<p>Her tişt&icirc; nake f&ecirc;hme</p>
<p>Av&ecirc; ji Xweda negre!</p>
<p>Tim qirac &ucirc; tim d&ecirc;me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ax&icirc;ret ebed&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Ev dinya j&icirc; fan&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Eva ku &ccedil;&icirc;kek av be</p>
<p>Ew behrek b&ecirc;bin&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew aql&ecirc; xwe dir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Ku tilyara bav&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Ji bo qurişa bimre</p>
<p>Ew k&icirc; be j&icirc; ew g&ecirc;j e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Axretfiroş pir ker e</p>
<p>Ji şeytan ra leşker e</p>
<p>Gerd&ucirc;n j&icirc; pehn l&ecirc; dixe</p>
<p>Qazanc nake tu pere</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gelo aqil k&icirc;ja ye</p>
<p>Ne ji koma g&ecirc;ja ye</p>
<p>Alv&ecirc;ra xwe rind dike</p>
<p>M&ecirc;vanek&icirc; h&ecirc;ja ye.</p>

<h1>B&Ecirc;XWED&Icirc;T&Icirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kovarek Kurd&icirc; derket</p>
<p>Kurd l&ecirc; xwed&icirc; derneket</p>
<p>Ku ji xwe ra rast n&icirc;ne</p>
<p>H&ecirc; j&icirc; &ccedil;&ucirc; b&ecirc;qud&ucirc;m ket</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima qelem nagre dest</p>
<p>Qey qud&ucirc;m&ecirc; w&icirc; şikest</p>
<p>J&rsquo;ber derd&ecirc; nezaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ku ez binv&icirc;sim helbest</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez nizanim &ccedil;i b&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>Ji sefahet&ecirc; g&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>Bi qenc&icirc; ez tineme</p>
<p>B&rsquo;xirab&icirc; dest dir&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>N&ucirc;bihar gula bihar</p>
<p>Kul&icirc;lk didin &ccedil;&ecirc;re dar</p>
<p>Tu ewqas şir&icirc;n&icirc; j&icirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima ev gel li te sar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iya pale &ucirc; kaş in</p>
<p>Ji ber zilm&ecirc; em şaş in</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima kovar b&ecirc;kese</p>
<p>Qey&icirc; em tev nexwaş in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ca hişyar be v&ecirc; car&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bixw&icirc;ne N&ucirc;bihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Zilma koma dijmina</p>
<p>Bi p&ecirc;n&ucirc;s&ecirc; b&icirc;n xar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>N&ucirc;bihara &Icirc;slam&icirc;</p>
<p>J&ecirc; ra bibe sam&icirc;m&icirc;</p>
<p>Rebb&ecirc; Qadir&ecirc; Hef&icirc;z</p>
<p>Ji me ra bibe ham&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xweda me bike şiyar</p>
<p>Dost&ecirc; xwe ra bike yar</p>
<p>Ser v&ecirc; zilma b&ecirc; fem&icirc;</p>
<p>Dojeh&ecirc; j&icirc; neke bar</p>

<h1>EZ&Ecirc; B&Ecirc;BEXT</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>W&icirc;cdana min dinale</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;je ev &ccedil;i hale</p>
<p>Gelo tu şiyar nab&icirc;</p>
<p>Ev xewart&icirc; &ccedil;end sale</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&icirc;n&ecirc; xwe neb&ucirc;m xwed&icirc;</p>
<p>Kor b&ucirc;m min dijmin ned&icirc;</p>
<p>Ku ez ji ol d&ucirc;r ketim</p>
<p>Heliyam h&ecirc;d&icirc; h&ecirc;d&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&icirc;na Se&icirc;d neb&ucirc;m n&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Wek Silhedd&icirc;n neb&ucirc;m ş&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Dijmina ez xapandim</p>

<h1>LO MELA</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Melay&ecirc; min radibe ji mala M&icirc;rze ye, nav&ecirc; dayka w&icirc; N&ucirc;r&ecirc; ye, biray&ecirc;n w&icirc; Muhemmed &ucirc; Ebdulmec&icirc;d, kek&ecirc; w&icirc; Ebd&ucirc;llah, xw&icirc;şk&ecirc;n w&icirc; Mircan &ucirc; Xanim &ucirc; Durriye ye. Melay&ecirc; min bi temen pi&ccedil;&ucirc;ke s&ecirc;zde ye &ccedil;arde ye. Di welat&ecirc; Kurdistan&ecirc; da di ser Melay&ecirc; min ra alim tineye, ilm&ucirc; zaneb&ucirc;na Melay&ecirc; min pir z&ecirc;de ye, kesek&ecirc; bi xwe bawer be &icirc;cazet&ecirc; bide Melay&ecirc; min tineye, Melay&ecirc; min xelef&ecirc; Mewlana Xalid&ecirc; esra berya me ye. Lo lo lo&hellip;</p>

<h1>ŞER&Icirc;ET</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>XER&Icirc;B&Ecirc; ZEMAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pişt&icirc; p&ecirc;xember pişt&icirc; eshaban</p>

<p>D&ucirc; siltanan j&icirc; mizir zaliman</p>
<p>Zordest&icirc; kirin li ser misliman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew muvahh&icirc;din wan any&ecirc; &icirc;man</p>
<p>Wan qeb&ucirc;l nekir dost&ecirc; şeytanan</p>
<p>Ew in waris&ecirc; heq p&ecirc;xemberan</p>
<p>Ew mucedd&icirc;d&ecirc; şah&ecirc; aliman</p>

<p>Ew&icirc; hildab&ucirc; sunnet&ucirc; Quran</p>
<p>Bo azadiy&ecirc; ma b&ecirc; av b&ecirc; nan</p>
<p>W&icirc; ser&icirc; hilda li ber deccalan</p>

<p>Qiyamet n&ecirc;z&icirc;k ev axr&ecirc; zeman</p>
<p>Kete tehl&ucirc;k&ecirc; d&icirc;n nam&ucirc;s &icirc;man</p>
<p>Bo xelasiya hem&icirc; misliman</p>
<p>Se&icirc;dek rab&ucirc; ji nav Kurdistan</p>

<p>Kurd&icirc;t&icirc; rakir em man b&ecirc; ziman</p>
<p>W&icirc; jera kufr&ecirc; da me misliman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kafir xebit&icirc;n ku rakin Quran</p>
<p>Minafiqan j&icirc; tev destdane wan</p>
<p>Se&icirc;d&ecirc; Nors&ecirc; rab&ucirc; j&rsquo;nav Kurdan</p>
<p>Got yan heq&ecirc; be yan here ev can</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>N&ucirc;ra Quran&ecirc; weşande c&icirc;han</p>
<p>Ser&icirc; xarnekir li ber zordestan</p>
<p>Wi pir cefa d&icirc;t d&rsquo;heps&ucirc; z&icirc;ndan</p>
<p>Şikir r&ecirc; vekir ji bo mezl&ucirc;man</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Werin de werin werin misliman</p>
<p>Em rind fam bikin xer&icirc;b&ecirc; zeman</p>

<p>Ew&ecirc; ji me ra bibine derman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Ji hev hez bikin bi dil &ucirc; bi can</p>

<h1>JI K&Ecirc; RA B&Ecirc;JIM</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>DENGB&Ecirc;J&Icirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>MIN HIŞYAR BIKIN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; min j&rsquo;xew&ecirc; venabin</p>
<p>Malxiraban qet t&ecirc;r nabin</p>
<p>Gelo w&ecirc; hergav ewha bin</p>
<p>Werin h&ucirc;n min hişyar bikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zanim umr&ecirc;m pir hindik e</p>
<p>M&icirc;na toveke dendik e</p>
<p>Ku birize k&ecirc; &ccedil;i bike?</p>
<p>Werin h&ucirc;n min hişyar bikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hizk&icirc; cin b&icirc; hizk&icirc; per&icirc;</p>
<p>Hizk&icirc; saxb&icirc; hizk&icirc; mir&icirc;</p>

<p>Tilol dibim l&rsquo;ser k&ecirc;lekan</p>

<p>Werin h&ucirc;n min hişyar bikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>W&icirc;cdan&acirc; min tim digir&icirc;</p>

<p>Bi war&ecirc; xer&icirc;b da şandim</p>

<h1>BIZANIBE</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>AV</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hey av&ecirc; av&ecirc; av&ecirc;</p>

<p>Qije qija tav&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Li paşiya min gor e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Yek b&ecirc;kar yek feqe ye</p>

<h1>DERD &Ucirc; XWEZ&Icirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Li biny&ecirc; m&ecirc;rg &ucirc; zev&icirc;</p>
<h4>Dar &ucirc; dirik &ucirc; dev&icirc;</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ser&ecirc; &ccedil;iya sip&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&Icirc;ro em b&ecirc; xwed&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji ber derd&ecirc; d&icirc;rok&ecirc;</p>

<h1>DAY&Icirc;K</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>SEYDAY&Ecirc; &Icirc;ZZEDD&Icirc;N</h1><p><br>Min r&icirc;sala xwe hilda</p>

<p>Pir cefa kişand Bed&icirc;uzzeman</p>
<p>Bona azad be alema &Icirc;slam</p>
<p>Ji şakirdan ra teral&icirc; nabe</p>
<p>Te helal nake tefs&icirc;ra Quran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ecirc;je ya Allah rabe serbixwe</p>
<p>Li c&icirc;han&ecirc; belavke doza xwe</p>
<p>Tu waris&ecirc; Roniya &ccedil;awan &icirc; (s.)</p>
<p>Xebatke raz&icirc; ke Xweday&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev n&ucirc;r n&ucirc;ra ew Xweday&ecirc; Semed</p>
<p>Em xadim&ecirc; w&ecirc; ne heta ebed</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>HEC&Icirc; &lsquo;EBDULLAH</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kal&ecirc; k&icirc; heye li Salor&icirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li mal dim&icirc;ne tev&ecirc; p&icirc;rek&ecirc;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;r&ecirc; du jina l&ecirc; b&ecirc; zuryet e</p>
<p>Din&ecirc; da ned&icirc;t ewlad &ucirc; b&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah</p>
<p>Al&icirc;kar&ecirc; te be Reh&icirc;m Allah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pirr&icirc; kal b&ucirc;ye l&rsquo;piya nam&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Guh nabih&icirc;ze &ccedil;av j&icirc; nab&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Kes w&icirc; napirse ten&ecirc; dim&icirc;ne</p>
<p>L&ecirc; gund&icirc; hem&icirc; meriv&ecirc; w&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah</p>
<p>Al&icirc;kar&ecirc; te be Reh&icirc;m Allah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rihm &ucirc; şefqeta merfa rab&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; ser xwe hal&ecirc; ket&icirc; şab&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Hey gel&icirc; gund&icirc; hey gel&icirc; &icirc;nsan</p>
<p>Ka &icirc;nsaniyeta me &ccedil;ab&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah Hec&icirc; &lsquo;Ebdullah</p>
<p>Al&icirc;kar&ecirc; te be Reh&icirc;m Allah</p>

<h1>R&Ecirc;WIYO</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;Umir di&ccedil;e wek&icirc; av</p>
<p>Em di xewda dert&ecirc; tav</p>
<p>Hatina vir careke</p>
<p>Venagere kal &ucirc; bav</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tunene duh &ucirc; sib&ecirc;</p>
<p>K&ecirc; dib&ecirc; bila bib&ecirc;</p>
<p>&lsquo;Umir roja &icirc;ro ye</p>
<p>D&ucirc; s&rsquo;be j&icirc; heye neb&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dixwaz&icirc; neb&icirc; poşman</p>
<p>Xebatke bi dil &ucirc; can</p>
<p>R&ecirc;wiyo r&ecirc; dir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Tu bi xwe ra bibe nan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mirin&ecirc; neke jib&icirc;r</p>
<p>Xwe ra bist&icirc;ne tevd&icirc;r</p>
<p>Deva xwe rind gir&ecirc;de</p>
<p>Paş&ecirc; b&ecirc; Xweda teqd&icirc;r</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;van&icirc; li v&ecirc; der&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kan&ecirc; &icirc;nsan&ecirc;n ber&ecirc;</p>
<p>Tişt&ecirc; t&ecirc; bib&icirc; bigre</p>
<p>Xwe bar neke wek ker&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>&Icirc;RO &Icirc;N E</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li ser&ecirc; Bil&icirc;can&ecirc; berf bariye</p>
<p>Lo hevalo tu bi min neke henek &ucirc; yariye</p>
<p>Ew emanet&ecirc; mezin bar&ecirc; giran&ecirc; ku erd&ucirc; ezman &ccedil;iya hilnedab&ucirc;</p>
<p>Ev b&ecirc;&ccedil;ar&ecirc; zalim&ecirc; nezan ketiye bin&ecirc; w&icirc; bariye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo birako &icirc;ro &icirc;n e dem pay&icirc;z e</p>
<p>He&ccedil;y&ecirc; nim&ecirc;ja &icirc;n&ecirc; kirye bi k&ecirc;fe dil&ecirc; w&icirc; ez&icirc;z e</p>
<p>Min sieta nim&ecirc;j&ecirc; da r&ecirc;w&icirc;t&icirc; kir, nim&ecirc;j nekir</p>
<p>Ji ber v&icirc; derd&icirc; gunehkar im, bir&icirc;ndar im, dil&ecirc; min digr&icirc; dixe x&icirc;ze x&icirc;ze</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min ber&ecirc; xwe daye Kopa ş&ecirc;l&ucirc; Xirabşer&ecirc; ewr say&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Meha Receb&ecirc; ye b&ecirc; roj&icirc; me l&ecirc; bir&ccedil;&icirc; me dil&ecirc;m t&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Min got şof&ecirc;ro mole bide em nim&ecirc;j kin</p>
<p>Ne şof&ecirc;r &ucirc; ne r&ecirc;wiya guh neda min cava min nedan negotin gotina te &ccedil;iye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>ŞIVAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo şivano wey şivano</p>
<p>Ra&icirc;f li vira m&ecirc;vano</p>
<p>Tu nab&ecirc;j&icirc; Ra&icirc;f bira</p>
<p>Tu l&rsquo;viray&icirc; ka pez kano</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şivan m&icirc;ha di&ccedil;&ecirc;r&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Şiv di destda bil&ucirc;r n&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Kum xistiye nav &ccedil;av&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>Nab&ecirc;je r&ecirc;w&icirc; h&ucirc;n k&icirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez derbas b&ucirc;me ji pir&ecirc;</p>
<p>Şivan ketye tefekkur&ecirc;</p>
<p>Heval&ecirc; min li para man</p>
<p>Xez&ucirc;r &ucirc; xal tev&ecirc; bir&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şivan qet nake hoqe hoq</p>
<p>Ben&icirc;şt&ecirc; xwe dixe belboq</p>
<p>Pez&ecirc; w&icirc; h&ucirc;r h&ucirc;r di&ccedil;&ecirc;re</p>
<p>Ew naxwe qanok &ucirc; xandoq</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo r&ecirc;wiyo tu &ccedil;i dik&icirc;</p>
<p>B&ecirc;je temaşa k&ecirc; dik&icirc;</p>
<p>Heger tu Xweda nasnek&icirc;</p>
<p>Tu ne spehiy&icirc;, sik&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez şivan im ez şivan im</p>
<p>Şivanek&icirc; b&ecirc; heban im</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; herme ber pez&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>Li v&icirc; gund&icirc; ez m&ecirc;van im</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez derketime li ser r&ecirc;</p>
<p>H&ecirc;v&icirc; dikim ku dolm&icirc;ş b&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dixwazim hetan&icirc; sib&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xwe bigh&icirc;nim ber guhur&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ker&icirc; li &ccedil;iy&ecirc; mexele</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; gura pir zexel e</p>
<p>Ley&icirc;stok&ecirc; naley&icirc;zim</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; diley&icirc;ze dexel e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pez&ecirc; min li Solor&icirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Balt&ucirc;z &ucirc; lawik &ucirc; b&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li h&ecirc;viya Xwed&ecirc; mane</p>
<p>Ez li v&ecirc; gaz &ucirc; gid&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Birr &icirc;ro b&ecirc; şivan maye</p>
<p>Gur hişyar e se raza ye</p>
<p>M&icirc;h &ucirc; bizin belav b&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>Tune d&ucirc;ajo winda ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ya Reb şivan b&icirc;ne ber pez</p>
<p>Pez nekeve nav heram rez</p>
<p>D&ucirc;ajok&icirc; tu biş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bi &icirc;zna te şivan im ez</p>

<h1>RIHA</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&Icirc;brah&icirc;m Xel&icirc;l &ccedil;&ecirc;tir e</p>

<h1>&lsquo;EL&Icirc; EZHER</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;El&icirc; Ezher gula zer</p>
<p>Şiyar b&ucirc; wext&ecirc; seher</p>
<p>Ji dinyay&ecirc; h&icirc;cret kir</p>
<p>W&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;kir seyr&ucirc; sefer</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nefsa xwe kir hesp &ucirc; ker</p>
<p>L&ecirc; siyar b&ucirc; derkete der</p>
<p>Ne ji &lsquo;evd&ecirc; fan&icirc; ra</p>
<p>Rebb&ecirc; xwe ra b&ucirc; nefer</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Te j&rsquo;b&icirc;r nakim lo Ezher</p>
<p>Biray&ecirc; te dikin şer</p>
<h5>Ez ketim nav&ccedil;&icirc;tiy&ecirc;</h5>
<p>L&rsquo;mi xistin şikandin ser</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez ji wan ra nabim per</p>
<p>Pir dim&icirc;nim şeve der</p>
<p>Tu bibe per bibe bask</p>
<p>Ji bo hevra nekin şer</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gund&icirc; pir dib&ecirc;jin &ccedil;er</p>
<p>Hinek j&icirc; dib&ecirc;jin wer</p>
<p>Ez dib&ecirc;m &ccedil;ak&icirc; wisa</p>
<p>Hewara me p&ecirc;xember</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu here cem p&ecirc;xember</p>
<p>Bila dua bike her</p>
<p>Seva em bibin meriv</p>
<p>Nebin k&ucirc;&ccedil;ik nebin ker</p>

<h1>TIŞTE NAY&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gozel&ecirc; bis&ecirc; denga gaz&icirc; dikir digot lo &lsquo;Imrano</p>
<p>Berx&ecirc; te &Icirc;shan&ecirc; te girtye t&ecirc;jk&ecirc; gurano</p>
<p>Biriye av&ecirc;tiye bin&ecirc; kul&ecirc; li heps&ecirc; li zindano</p>
<p>Tu rabe here d&icirc;tin&ecirc; nizanim t&icirc; ye yan bir&ccedil;&icirc; ye j&ecirc; ra bibe av &ucirc; nano</p>
<p>Ez pep&ucirc;kim kevne jinim dara şikest&icirc;me ji dest&ecirc; min tişte nay&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&lsquo;Imran dib&ecirc; l&ecirc; Gozel&ecirc; l&ecirc; heval&ecirc; l&ecirc; delal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Tu berx&ecirc; xwe xwey&icirc;ke bisekine li nav mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nim&ecirc;j bike ji Rebb&ecirc; mezin ra bike kale kal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; berx&ecirc; xwe mezin kin hetan&icirc; ser&ecirc; sal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez &lsquo;evdal im kale m&ecirc;rim B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me ji dest&ecirc; min tişte nay&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Jiyan dib&ecirc; l&ecirc; day&ecirc; lo bavo wiha nabe</p>
<p>Doza azadiy&ecirc; b&ecirc; xebat &ucirc; b&ecirc; biha &ccedil;&ecirc;nabe</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; biha bidin bila gel ji xewa giran rabe</p>
<p>Bila xelq&ecirc; me azad be li ser axa xwe dilşabe</p>
<p>Ez pi&ccedil;&ucirc;k im ne pep&ucirc;k im h&ecirc;v&icirc;dar im ji dest&ecirc; min tişte nay&ecirc;</p>

<h1>USTAD&Ecirc; MIN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<h4>Ez&ecirc; bi geliy&ecirc; Bil&icirc;s&ecirc; diketim lo pir bi ave</h4>
<p>Zivistane berf bariye hewa germ e li me dixe roj &ucirc; tave</p>
<p>Bil&icirc;s bajar&ecirc; Seyday&ecirc; min e bi nav&ecirc; ş&ecirc;r&icirc;n Bed&icirc;uzzeman Se&icirc;d&ecirc; Kurd&icirc; li bajar&ecirc; Bil&icirc;s&ecirc; nav&ccedil;a H&icirc;zan&ecirc; gund&ecirc; Nors&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; daye d&ecirc;y&ucirc; bave</p>
<p>Ez tu car ustad&ecirc; xwe j&rsquo;b&icirc;r nakim ez&ecirc; kit&ecirc;b&ecirc; w&icirc; bixw&icirc;nim di r&ecirc;ya w&icirc; ya delal da bajom bav&ecirc;jim ling &ucirc; gave.</p>
<p>Ustad&ecirc; min Seyday&ecirc; min Delal&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo ustado te mala xwe bar kir tu &ccedil;&ucirc;y&icirc; heqiy&ecirc; em mane li v&ecirc; dinya han&ecirc;</p>
<p>Medresa te ya Zehra n&ecirc;v&icirc; maye Mele &Icirc;zzed&icirc;n şeh&icirc;d kirin dijminane</p>
<p>Şakird&ecirc; te razane xew ş&ecirc;r&icirc;n e xew da mane</p>
<p>Ez &ccedil;i bikim ez nikarim şiyar bikim B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me r&ecirc; nas nakim nizanim şiyarkirin &ccedil;awane</p>
<p>Ustad&ecirc; min Seyday&ecirc; min Delal&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ser&ecirc; &ccedil;iy&ecirc; bi mije d&icirc;sa bi d&ucirc;mane</p>
<p>Sube z&ucirc; ye m&ecirc;van di xewdane sare h&ecirc; veneb&ucirc;ne dikane</p>
<p>Welat&ecirc; me Serhed e hav&icirc;n&ecirc; h&ecirc;nike zozan e</p>
<p>&Icirc;ro berf bariye li me surre seqeme zemher&icirc;re em b&ecirc; mal in d&icirc;sa li me b&ucirc;ye serma &ucirc; zivistane</p>
<p>Ustad&ecirc; min Seyday&ecirc; min Delal&ecirc; min</p>

<h1>MERZEL&Ecirc; DAY&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Roja yekşem&ecirc; ez</p>
<p>Ne&ccedil;&ucirc;me liber pez</p>
<p>Bona d&icirc;tina day&ecirc;</p>
<p>Min gav av&ecirc;t lez bi lez</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Heta pez were dana</p>

<p>Ketim nav goristan&ecirc;</p>

<h1>BERX&Ecirc;M RAZ&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>ZAROK&Ecirc;N KURDAN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez dinh&ecirc;rim li Kurdistan<br>Dib&icirc;nim gellek zarokan</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; ku gavan y&ecirc; ku şivan<br>Y&ecirc; golikvan y&ecirc; ku berxvan</p>
<p>Ne li hundir tim li derin<br>Xebatkarin &ucirc; r&ecirc;ncberin</p>
<p>Hinek &ecirc; xwe hinek y&ecirc; din<br>Li derva r&ecirc;ncbery&ecirc; dikin</p>
<p>Ew di&ccedil;ine ber heywana<br>Pir na&ccedil;ine dibistana</p>
<p>B&ecirc; medrese b&ecirc; dibistan<br>Mezin dibin li ser &ccedil;iyan</p>
<p>Li ber pez &ucirc; garan&ecirc;ne<br>Li ber şily&ecirc; baran&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Ew nas dikin qolo hir&ccedil;o<br>Gajo, &ccedil;ilp&icirc; &ucirc; dar &ucirc; &ccedil;o</p>
<p>Zarok&ecirc; pir j&ecirc;hat&icirc;ne<br>L&ecirc; &ccedil;ibkim ew b&ecirc;xwed&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Qeliş&icirc;ne bin&ecirc; sola<br>P&ecirc; digerin deşt &ucirc; &ccedil;ola</p>
<p>Kinc&ecirc; wana perpit&icirc;ne<br>Gellek bir&ccedil;&icirc; gellek t&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Reş b&ucirc;ne ew li ber tav&ecirc;<br>B&ucirc;ne h&ecirc;s&icirc;r&ecirc; d&ecirc; bav&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xulamin bi meh &ucirc; sala<br>Nab&icirc;nin hundir&ecirc; mala</p>
<p>Nan &ucirc; toraq hinek p&icirc;vaz<br>Gir&ecirc;dane dane hevraz</p>
<p>Hevraz &ucirc; berj&ecirc;r digerin<br>D&ecirc;y&ucirc; bav&ecirc; wana kherin</p>
<p>Nabh&icirc;zin hewara wana<br>Ku biş&icirc;nin dibistana</p>
<p>Bo ew h&icirc;n bibin xwendin&ecirc;<br>Xwendin &ucirc; niv&icirc;sandin&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xilas bin ji gavaniy&ecirc;<br>Ji paşmay&icirc;n, nezaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Azad bin jifeq&icirc;riy&ecirc;<br>Ji ket&icirc;t&icirc;, heq&icirc;riy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bila mezin bibin şivan<br>Gavan, berxvan &ucirc; golikvan</p>
<p>Pez&ecirc; xwe t&ecirc;xin tev şivan<br>Berx&ecirc; xwe bikin tev berxvan</p>
<p>Golika bidin golikvan<br>Dewara t&ecirc;xin ber gavan</p>
<p>Ku zarok&ecirc; me bixw&icirc;nin<br>Tehs&icirc;l bikin binv&icirc;s&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Zarok&ecirc; me pir gunene<br>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; wan li dest&ecirc; mene</p>
<p>Em cahilin paşda mane<br>Qenebe zar bibin zane</p>

<h1>HESRET</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji sub&ecirc; heta &ecirc;var&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dikş&icirc;nim hesreta yar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bona miraz&ecirc; me bike</p>
<p>J&rsquo;Yezdan dixwazim hewar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Yara min yeke sal&icirc;he</p>
<p>Ziman xweşe hem Mel&icirc;he</p>
<p>Ji tirsa eşkere nakim</p>
<p>Bi ten&ecirc; dikim telm&icirc;he</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bo xwastina heval&ecirc;</p>
<p>D&ucirc;r ketime ez ji mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez hesreta rind&ecirc; mame</p>
<p>Roj&ecirc; min b&ucirc;n weke sal&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Deng &ucirc; awazam Zehra ye</p>
<p>Her gav doza min Zehra ye</p>
<p>Heta li din&ecirc; bim&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Yar &ucirc; daxwazam Zehra ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gula min sore &ccedil;&icirc;&ccedil;eke</p>
<p>Xweda bext&ecirc; gulam veke</p>
<p>Nav gul&icirc;stana gula da</p>
<p>Gulam ji gulan guleke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez mame hesreta gul&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dizarim wek&icirc; bilbil&ecirc;</p>
<p>Miraz&ecirc; min gul&ecirc; bibe</p>
<p>Razim&ecirc; bgaris gilgil&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gulam guleke reng&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bi dil&ecirc; xwe pir zeng&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Şekir&icirc;ne hingiv&icirc;ne</p>
<p>L&ecirc; dertg&icirc;ran, xemg&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc;m dixwaze w&icirc;sale</p>
<p>L&ecirc; B&ecirc;&ccedil;are ye &lsquo;evdale</p>
<p>H&ecirc;v&icirc; lava j&rsquo;Xweda dike</p>
<p>Ku z&ucirc;tir yar were male</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>M&Icirc;RZE MUHEMMED</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>

<h5>Tu lku may&icirc; M&icirc;rze Muhemmed</h5>

<p>&Ecirc;r&icirc;şkir d&ecirc;w&ecirc; şeş ser&icirc;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mala Derw&ecirc;ş li M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Dike dikanvaniy&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tev&ecirc; &Ucirc;sb&ecirc; bir&ecirc; Weys&icirc;</p>
<p>Difroşin birinc&ucirc; qeys&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mihme Nur&icirc; tev&ecirc; Ekrem</p>
<p>Ji gund derketin &ccedil;em bi &ccedil;em</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bav&ecirc; wan mir roja &icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ew hatine dikin ş&icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Feq&icirc;r in ehl&ecirc; x&ecirc;ran e</p>
<p>L&ecirc; xurt in cisn&ecirc; ş&ecirc;rane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ap&ecirc; Şukr&icirc; bav&ecirc; wan e</p>
<p>Pişta xwe da dinya hane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; l&ecirc; bike rehmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ef&ucirc;ke bixe cennet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em ji Xweda h&ecirc;v&icirc;dar in</p>
<p>Him feq&icirc;rin him b&ecirc;&ccedil;ar in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez Ra&icirc;f&ecirc; B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me</p>
<p>Bejn kinik im eware me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez ne mele H&ucirc;sey&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Mamostek&icirc; del &ucirc; d&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwe b&rsquo;helbesta dixap&icirc;nim</p>
<p>B&ecirc;na xwe we p&ecirc; dert&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Peyay&ecirc; mala Mexso me</p>
<p>Birazy&ecirc; şivan Silho me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xilamy&ecirc; me Nuredd&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Ap&ecirc; Selim Şemsedd&icirc;n e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Birayek&icirc; w&icirc; Cemal e</p>
<p>Ap&ecirc; Mehm&ucirc;d&ecirc; &lsquo;Evdal e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bir&ecirc; Hec&icirc; Mika&icirc;l e</p>
<p>Bi me b&ucirc; raz&icirc; qa&icirc;l e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Q&icirc;za xwe da Xirabşer&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xweda b&rsquo;x&ecirc;rke v&ecirc; qeder&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ucirc;ye b&ucirc;ka Salh&ecirc; M&icirc;rze</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; w&ecirc; neke şepirze</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; s&rsquo;yar be kera mih&icirc;na</p>
<p>Here bişkula serg&icirc;na</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew xelg&ecirc; Gely&ecirc; Z&icirc;lan in</p>
<p>&Icirc;ro l&rsquo;&ccedil;iyay&ecirc; Bil&icirc;can in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew M&icirc;rzey&ecirc; M&icirc;rz&ecirc; Temo</p>
<p>Kalk&ecirc; Ra&icirc;f Cimo Remo</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kalik &ccedil;&ucirc;n dilovaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Em mane li ser xaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; xan&icirc; ava bike</p>
<p>Feh&icirc;m t&ecirc; da zava bike</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Feh&icirc;m zav&ecirc; v&icirc; gund&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Xwarzy&ecirc; Bekir&ecirc; &lsquo;El&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li Bekir be</p>
<p>Ş&icirc;va w&icirc; ş&icirc;r &ucirc; şekir be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gotye meriv bibe tey&icirc;b</p>
<p>Denga qeyd ke neke qey&icirc;b</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bibin radyo b&icirc;la &ecirc; din</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n bibin tey&icirc;b ber hildin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev gotina mezina ye</p>
<p>V&ecirc; nev&ecirc;jin pişt guha ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bidr&ucirc;n m&ecirc;rga &ucirc; g&icirc;ha ye</p>
<p>Pir r&ucirc;nen&ecirc;n li ber s&icirc;ha ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bidin emeg &ucirc; bihaye</p>
<p>T&ecirc;r bixwin toy&ecirc; m&icirc;haye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bila du bask&ecirc; we hebe</p>
<p>Yek aqil yek qelb&ecirc; we be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku h&ucirc;n bikarbin bifirin</p>
<p>Ber bi war&ecirc; xwe be herin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&ecirc; biaqile ne d&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Dizane li vir nam&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>L&ecirc; heta &ccedil;&ucirc;n&ecirc; mirin&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; &icirc;nsan li kirin&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em bikin wan kirin&ecirc;n qenc</p>
<p>Ku em paş&ecirc; xwe nekin penc</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em bixwin bidin &icirc;nsana</p>
<p>Bidin r&ecirc;wya &ucirc; m&ecirc;vana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bidin gavan &ucirc; şivana</p>
<p>R&ecirc;ncber berxvan golikvana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hav&icirc;n&ecirc; herin zozana</p>
<p>B&ecirc;n bikin gul &ucirc; rihana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi&ccedil;&ecirc;r&icirc;nin pir heywana</p>
<p>C&ecirc;jn&ecirc; da bidin qurbana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Guh bidine helbest vana</p>
<p>Sitranb&ecirc;j &ucirc; xweş hozana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bixwazin d&icirc;n &ucirc; &icirc;mana</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n pir bixw&icirc;nin Qurana</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xweday&ecirc; erd &ucirc; ezmana</p>
<p>Bide we horiy xilmana</p>

<h1>XEBATA QENAL&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em hatin gund&ecirc; Afyon&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bona bibin per&ecirc; non&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; me n&ecirc;v&icirc; da ma ye</p>
<p>Dikim nakim na&ccedil;e son&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5>Heval&ecirc; min xelq&ecirc; P&icirc;ran</h5>
<p>Betal mane li gund&ecirc; han</p>
<p>Ez ji Xwed&ecirc; h&ecirc;v&icirc; dikim</p>
<p>Rihm&ecirc; bike l&rsquo;me h&ecirc;s&icirc;ran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek&ecirc; Hem&icirc;d &ucirc; xal&ecirc; min</p>
<p>Tev&ecirc; &ccedil;arde heval&ecirc; min</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; wana li r&ecirc; na&ccedil;e</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;jin &ccedil;abe hal&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; &ccedil;ab&rsquo;kim betoner&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xirab b&ucirc;ye li ser&ecirc; r&ecirc;</p>
<p>Herro me şepirze dike</p>
<p>Em b&ucirc;ne &lsquo;evdal&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em ketine nav qenal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li ber germ&ecirc; l&rsquo;v&ecirc; newal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; pere qezenc bikin</p>
<p>Ji bo aboriya mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li vir em dib&icirc;nin cefa</p>
<p>Me l&rsquo;d&icirc;nyay&ecirc; nedit wefa</p>
<p>Tirsa min a mezin ew e</p>
<p>Axret&ecirc; tunebe sefa</p>

<h1>DERS</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ra&icirc;f &ucirc; &lsquo;El&icirc; &Icirc;zzet</p>
<p>Sib&ecirc; z&ucirc; ji mal derket</p>
<p>Gotin ji me hereket</p>
<p>Ji Xweda j&icirc; bereket</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;&ucirc;n ku herin medres&ecirc;</p>
<p>Guhdar&icirc; bikin ders&ecirc;</p>
<p>Diya &lsquo;El&icirc; biray&ecirc;n w&icirc;</p>
<p>Li mal dim&icirc;nin hers&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew dim&icirc;nin li mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xaltiy&ecirc; were bal&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; wan li r&ecirc; ma ye</p>
<p>Sal hate ser&ecirc; sal&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şakirde &lsquo;El&icirc; Izzet</p>
<p>Seyday&ecirc; w&icirc; şeh&icirc;d ket</p>
<p>Bi pi&ccedil;&ucirc;ktiya xweba</p>
<p>Li doz&ecirc; xwey&icirc; derket</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rab&ucirc;ye ser kurs&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Doza seyda pirs&icirc; ye</p>
<p>De&rsquo;wa Mele Izzedd&icirc;n</p>
<p>Doza Se&icirc;d N&ucirc;rs&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo dersa heq&icirc;qet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Min h&icirc;şt zarok w&icirc; h&icirc;şt d&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ji bo da&icirc;m xizmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; bide taqet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo em nefs&ecirc; islah kin</p>
<p>Ji agir&ecirc; xelas kin</p>
<p>K&icirc;jan r&ecirc; xweşe raste</p>
<p>Li dinyay&ecirc; em naskin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>&lsquo;ELBIHAR</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>V&ecirc; demsal&ecirc; bihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;&ucirc;m jor nehatim xar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bo seyda Mele Kerem</p>
<p>Hatim Ewilbihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ewilbihare gund e</p>
<h5>Him &ccedil;ele him bilind e</h5>
<p>Nav gund&ecirc; dorh&ecirc;l&ecirc; da</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iqas gundek&icirc; rind e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez tev&ecirc; Mele Kerem</p>
<p>J&rsquo;mal derketin esirdem</p>
<p>Him &ccedil;&ucirc;n nav goristan&ecirc;</p>
<p>Him j&icirc; me seyr kirin &ccedil;em</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me li gund kire seyran</p>
<p>Em j&ecirc;ra b&ucirc;ne heyran</p>
<p>Ku bask&ecirc; me heb&ucirc;na</p>
<p>Em difir&icirc;n wek teyran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Roj xweş e li bihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Di v&ecirc; meha adar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Roja berya newroz&ecirc;</p>
<p>Min kirye terka yar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Elbihar Ewwilbihar</p>
<p>Bi m&ecirc;rg &ucirc; zev&icirc; bi dar</p>
<p>&Icirc;sal ez hatim vira</p>
<p>Min ned&icirc;b&ucirc; sala par</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me mala mele nan xwar</p>
<p>B&ucirc; &ecirc;var li me b&ucirc; sar</p>
<p>H&ecirc; ne&ccedil;ib&ucirc;m Zorava</p>
<p>Hewandib&ucirc;n pez &ucirc; kar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>P&ecirc;yat&icirc; di&ccedil;&ucirc;me mal</p>
<p>Ez ten&ecirc; me b&ecirc; heval</p>
<p>Li ser van r&ecirc; y&ucirc; dirba</p>
<p>H&ecirc; j&icirc; xort im neb&ucirc;m kal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&ucirc;r im ji ap &ucirc; ji xal</p>
<p>Neg&icirc;h&icirc;şt&icirc;me l&ecirc; kal</p>
<p>Par li Salor&icirc;k&ecirc; b&ucirc;m</p>
<p>Hatim Zorava &icirc;sal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hatina me bi x&ecirc;r be</p>
<p>Heval&ecirc; me cam&ecirc;r be</p>
<p>Di r&ecirc;ya jiyan&ecirc; da</p>
<p>Dost&ecirc; me &lsquo;El&icirc;ş&ecirc;r be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>MAMOST&Ecirc;N ZORAVA</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira Bahadd&icirc;n Akdaş</p>
<p>Li Zorava dibe kaş</p>
<p>Ji m&ecirc;ra ra j&icirc; baş e</p>
<p>Le ji jina ra zaf baş</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwişkeke min Elvan e</p>
<p>&Icirc;sal li vir m&ecirc;vane</p>
<p>Reng reng&icirc; dixemile</p>
<p>Ew miriy&ecirc; rengane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>L&ecirc; xwişka min e Hewa</p>
<p>Mezin e m&icirc;na d&ecirc;wa</p>
<p>Bejn bilind e dir&ecirc;j e</p>
<p>Meriv j&ecirc; digre sawa</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hewa xelq&ecirc; M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>M&icirc;na hespeke ş&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Yeke reş e qemer e</p>
<p>Nizam ne &ccedil;&ecirc; yan &ccedil;&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>S&ecirc; heval mamostene</p>
<p>Dersa xwe da hostane</p>
<p>&Icirc;lim didin zaroka</p>
<p>Direş&icirc;nin bostane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;n hatiye bihar</p>
<p>Me ra b&ucirc;ye dost &ucirc; yar</p>
<p>L&ecirc; min ew ned&icirc;tiye</p>
<p>Nizam xurte yan j&icirc; jar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bad&icirc;n ber&ecirc; heval e</p>
<p>Merivek&icirc; delal e</p>
<p>Pir&icirc; ku ders&ecirc; dide</p>
<p>Ew dereng di&ccedil;e male</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Elvan ji roava ye</p>
<p>H&ecirc; neditye zavaye</p>
<p>Ji welat&ecirc; xwe d&ucirc;r e</p>
<p>Ke&ccedil;a d&ecirc;y&ucirc; bava ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez Ra&icirc;f B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me</p>
<p>Ji dila parpare me</p>
<p>B&ecirc;halim peşm&ucirc;rde me</p>
<p>L&rsquo;dinyay&ecirc; eware me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>EZ &Ucirc; EW</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez M&ecirc;rk&ecirc; peya ew m&ecirc;rk&ecirc; siwar&icirc;</p>
<p>Ez m&ecirc;rk&ecirc; gund&icirc; ew y&ecirc; bajar&icirc;</p>
<p>Ez y&ecirc; sibey&icirc; ew y&ecirc; &ecirc;var&icirc;</p>
<p>Bi wira ez&ecirc; &ccedil;a bav&ecirc;jim gav?</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez xelq&ecirc; gund im li ber germ&ecirc; me</p>
<p>Ew b&ecirc; fed&icirc; ez xwey&ecirc; şerm&ecirc; me</p>
<p>Ew bi qal&icirc;fer in ez ber kerm&ecirc; me</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; bi wan ra &ccedil;a bibim heval</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew meden&icirc; ne ez bedew&icirc; me</p>
<p>Pişta wan xurt e l&ecirc; ez s&ecirc;w&icirc; me</p>
<p>Ew herro t&ecirc;r in ez bir&ccedil;&icirc; t&icirc; me</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; bi wan ra &ccedil;a bibim hemhal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew didin jina merhebatiy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Him raz&icirc; b&ucirc;ne bi tez&icirc;tiy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez napejr&icirc;n im b&ecirc;x&icirc;retiy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ava min wana &ccedil;a dibe zelal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; wan h&ecirc;z e y&ecirc; min j&icirc; heq e</p>
<p>Lord dibe heqdar feq&icirc;r niheq e</p>
<p>Ji ber zilma wan were neteqe</p>
<p>Li ber niheqa &ccedil;a bibim &lsquo;evdal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez kurmanc im ew hem&icirc; rom&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Ez ten&ecirc; mame ew kom kom&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Şuxl&ecirc; wan şerab xumar dom&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; li wana &ccedil;awa bidim pal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi pol &ucirc; peraba ew serxoş in</p>
<p>Bo menfeet&ecirc; min difiroşin</p>
<p>Tasa min tune ew bi beroş in</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; ji wan ra &ccedil;a b&ecirc;jim delal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em cins&ecirc; ş&ecirc;ra ew cins&ecirc; gura</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; ji wan ra &ccedil;a bibim bira</p>
<p>Xay&icirc;n med&rsquo;kujin l&rsquo;ber av &ucirc; pira</p>
<p>Em&ecirc; maf&ecirc; xwe &ccedil;a bikin helal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>B&Icirc;RAN&Icirc;NEK RIHAY&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira bira werin vira</p>
<p>Em ji hevra bibin bira</p>
<p>Nev&ecirc;jine hev kevira</p>
<p>Em fesal&ecirc; nedin gura</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Riha medresa zehra ye</p>
<p>Merqeda Ustad t&ecirc; da ye</p>
<p>Ciy&ecirc; p&icirc;r p&ecirc;xembera ye</p>
<p>Ev ne war&ecirc; Nemr&ucirc;da ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li Rihay&ecirc; em bidin soz</p>
<p>Doza Seyda em bikin doz</p>
<p>Hildin em w&ecirc; doza p&icirc;roz</p>
<p>Mirina me cejna newroz</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xel&icirc;l &Icirc;brah&icirc;m li vira</p>
<p>P&ucirc;t şikandin bi bivira</p>
<p>Ew av&ecirc;tin nav agira</p>
<p>Agir b&ucirc; av ew b&ucirc; &ccedil;ira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n dizanin ka em k&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Em s&ecirc;wiy&ecirc; ummet&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Em &Icirc;slam in li ser r&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Ke&ccedil; &ucirc; xort&ecirc; bav &ucirc; d&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bav&ecirc; me Adem baba ye</p>
<p>Dayka me diya Hewa ye</p>
<p>Qibla meya mum&icirc;na ye</p>
<p>P&icirc;r&ecirc; me dost&ecirc; Xweda ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kalk&ecirc; me Selahedd&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Seyday&ecirc; me &Icirc;zzedd&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Ustad&ecirc; me bib&icirc;r b&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ew Se&icirc;d&ecirc; nav şir&icirc;n e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bikin tobe bibin poşman</p>
<p>Paqij bibin ji gunehan</p>
<p>Rind bigirin bend&ecirc; Quran</p>
<p>Yezdan&ecirc; me pir dilovan</p>
