<h1>DU MALIK</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Aqil&ecirc; d&icirc;na</p>
<p>D&ecirc;lb&ecirc;jy&ecirc; mih&icirc;na</p>
<p>P&ecirc; bendik &ccedil;&ecirc;ke</p>
<p>Gir&ecirc;de z&icirc;na</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Aqil&ecirc; bi aqila</p>
<p>Bav&ecirc;je &ccedil;akila</p>
<p>Qalika j&ecirc; derxe</p>
<p>Bip&icirc;ve kakila</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>BILATIXA HEV&Ecirc;DYAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bilatixa Hev&ecirc;dya ye</p>
<p>Bilinde gund&ecirc; &ccedil;iya ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rojek &ccedil;&ucirc;me Bilatix&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ketim nav qelebalix&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Qelebalixa zara b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Bay&ecirc; Kurdo li me rab&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me yek&icirc;t&icirc; rind &ccedil;&ecirc;nekir</p>
<p>Bilatix&ecirc; zora me bir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h4>Xas&icirc;k gundek m&icirc;na ş&ecirc;r b&ucirc;</h4>
<p>Me zora Xas&icirc;k&ecirc; birb&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bilatix bi wan nikar b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Bi wan ra beramber mab&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Felek ji me ra rast neb&ucirc;</p>
<p>Qeledar&ecirc; me tune b&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nehatib&ucirc; &ccedil;ib&ucirc; zozan</p>
<p>Li zozana bib&ucirc; berxvan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Sib&ecirc; z&ucirc; ez di xew da b&ucirc;m</p>
<p>Ji nim&ecirc;j&ecirc; paşda mab&ucirc;m</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ten&ecirc; hatib&ucirc;n l&icirc;stikvan</p>
<p>Em mab&ucirc;n b&ecirc; temaşevan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; nehatin nifira kir</p>
<p>Me eva ma&ccedil;a winda kir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me windakir ka &ccedil;i bikim</p>
<p>Bilatix&ecirc; p&icirc;roz dikim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Meriv ji meriv z&ecirc;de ye</p>
<p>Pişt&icirc; &ecirc;var&ecirc; sibe ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc;jin gerd&ucirc;n bi dor e</p>
<p>Carek li j&ecirc;r yek li jor e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Peyat&icirc; dihatim xam b&ucirc;m</p>
<p>Ji Xas&icirc;k&ecirc; ra pismam b&ucirc;m</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li mala Hec&icirc; &Icirc;sma&icirc;l</p>
<p>Ew xam b&ucirc;n ji min b&ucirc; za&icirc;l</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;sma&icirc;l baş e cam&ecirc;r e</p>
<p>Berder&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;dike k&ecirc;r e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>W&ecirc; g&icirc;ha bidr&ucirc; bi k&ecirc;r&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ji mal&ecirc; ra bike x&ecirc;r&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kur&ecirc; Reş&icirc;t&ecirc; Fet&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Xas&icirc;k&ecirc; da li ber r&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;van m&ecirc;van&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>J&ecirc; ra dike xizmet&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dide &ccedil;ay&ecirc; ava meyva</p>
<p>Mij&ucirc;l dibe xweş peyiva</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez &ucirc; ew ji malek&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Ji zuryeta kalek&icirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav&ecirc; bav&ecirc; me Resa ye</p>
<p>Kal&ecirc; me teva Mexso ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Heft kur&ecirc; Mexso heb&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>Yek ji yek&icirc; z&ecirc;de b&ucirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Reso kirye terka Motkan</p>
<p>Ji wir &ccedil;&ucirc;ye Gely&ecirc; Z&icirc;lan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; da zar&ecirc; me kuştin</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; f&icirc;rar b&ucirc;n ewna hiştin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez ser&ecirc; we di&ecirc;ş&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Reşgir&ecirc;didim biş&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; li me dike ş&icirc;ret</p>
<p>Ew&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;kirne eş&icirc;ret</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bo meriv hevd&ucirc; nas kin</p>
<p>Jiyana xwe rind derbas kin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ne ji bona neyartiy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ji bona al&icirc;kartiy&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>ZEHRADIL</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu gula dil&ecirc; min&icirc; ey Zehradil</p>
<p>H&ecirc;sra nebar&icirc;ne &ccedil;ava neke şil</p>
<p>Wa bihara welat&ecirc; me hatiye</p>
<p>Ew zeviy&ecirc; &ccedil;andine dibin simbil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zehra leqeb&ecirc; hezret Fatima ye</p>
<h4>Fatima xat&ucirc;na hem&icirc; jina ye</h4>
<p>Q&icirc;za dayka me Xed&icirc;ca Kubra ye</p>
<p>Ke&ccedil;a p&ecirc;xember&ecirc; ronya &ccedil;ava ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu xwuşk&icirc; kek&ecirc; te ye &lsquo;El&icirc; Ezher</p>
<p>Dersa xwe bixw&icirc;ne rind bike ezber</p>
<p>&lsquo;El&icirc; Ezher b&ucirc; zad&ecirc; ax&icirc;ret&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xatir ji me xwest &ccedil;&ucirc; cem Rebb&ecirc; Ekber</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav&ecirc; te nav&ecirc; w&ecirc; gula Zehra ye</p>
<p>Wesyeta seyda ye gelek h&ecirc;ja ye</p>
<p>Bed&icirc;uzzeman ji bon&ecirc; xebitye</p>
<p>Ew lazim d&icirc;tye ji bo me Kurda ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Medresa Zehra &icirc;ro &ccedil;&ecirc;neb&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Seyday&ecirc; me &Icirc;zzedd&icirc;n şeh&icirc;d b&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Şakird&ecirc; w&icirc; &icirc;ro b&ecirc; ser&icirc; mane</p>
<p>Şiyar nabin ku bidine d&ucirc; w&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez w&ecirc; di dil&ecirc; xwe da di&ccedil;ik&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Min ew ava nekir ez dil bir&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Loma min nav&ecirc; te danye Zehradil</p>
<p>Qenebe dil&ecirc; xwe da w&ecirc; bib&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ecirc;viya min ji w&icirc; Rebb&ecirc; &Icirc;zzet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Şakirda şiyarke b&icirc;ne x&icirc;ret&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ku w&ecirc; medresa Zehra ava bikin</p>
<p>Ji xelq &ucirc; Xaliq ra bikin xizmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dijmina pir li ser te kir pilepil</p>
<p>Ew ji nav&ecirc; te ditirse dibe sil</p>
<p>X&ecirc;rnexaz ji weca te bibecin j&icirc;</p>
<p>Tu bixemle &ccedil;av&ecirc; belek bike kil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; qedr&ecirc; te nizane b&ucirc;ye xafil</p>
<p>Şiyar nake rih &ucirc; dil tev&ecirc; aqil</p>
<p>H&ecirc;v&icirc; dikim Xweda wan ji xew rake</p>
<p>Berbi qenciy&ecirc;va bike tehewwil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji Xweda y&ecirc; mezin w&icirc; Rebb&ecirc; Adil</p>
<p>Dixwazim ji dawiy&ecirc; heta ewwil</p>
<p>Li ser rastiy&ecirc; me bike wek bilbil</p>
<p>Em yek&icirc;tiya xwe &ccedil;&ecirc;kin mil bi mil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>KANYA B&Ucirc;K&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ucirc;k&ecirc; day&icirc;ka Kemal e</p>
<p>&lsquo;Umr&ecirc; w&ecirc; ş&ecirc;st heft&ecirc; sal e</p>
<p>Malx&ecirc; w&ecirc; wefat kirye</p>
<p>Ew h&ecirc;ji b&ucirc;k e bermal e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>P&icirc;re reben&ecirc; pep&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Gund&icirc; j&ecirc;ra dib&ecirc;n b&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li Kurdzoravay&ecirc; dij&icirc;</p>
<p>Roj&acirc; meaş di&ccedil;e s&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kanya mala me tuneye</p>
<p>L&ecirc; kaniya b&ucirc;k&ecirc; heye</p>
<p>Nav&ecirc; w&ecirc; l&rsquo;ser kaniy&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Ava kany&ecirc; pir z&ecirc;de ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kan&icirc; ji me ra rehmet e</p>
<p>Kur&ecirc; w&ecirc; Hakim N&icirc;met e</p>
<p>&Ecirc; din Menderes &ucirc; Şakir</p>
<p>Li M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; dikin xebat e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dayka p&ecirc;nc kur s&ecirc; q&icirc;za ye</p>
<p>P&icirc;rka gund e ya gela ye</p>
<p>Bi nav&ecirc; xwe Gulpaşa ye</p>
<p>M&ecirc;ran&icirc; ye pir h&ecirc;ja ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi x&icirc;ret e pir bi kar e</p>
<p>Pir ranaz&ecirc; zaf şiyar e</p>
<p>Dormal&ecirc; r&ecirc;ncbery&ecirc; dike</p>
<p>Ber golik hesp &ucirc; dewar e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>ENES</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav&ecirc; v&icirc; xort&icirc; Enes e</p>
<p>Ew lawik&ecirc; Menderes e</p>
<p>Aly&ecirc; min av&ecirc; dikş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ji min ra biray&ecirc; kes e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di&ccedil;e sinifa sis&ecirc;ya</p>
<p>Kety&ecirc; nava j&icirc;r &ucirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;ya</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; hezke y&ecirc; bixw&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Şa bike bav xwişk &ucirc; d&ecirc;ya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwendina xwe da ji dil e</p>
<p>Zarokek&icirc; bi aqil e</p>
<p>Ji bona p&ecirc;şda&ccedil;&ucirc;y&icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>Div&ecirc;t hilde zend &ucirc; mile</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>ZOZAN&Ecirc; XAN&Icirc;KER&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zozan&ecirc; Xan&icirc;ker&ecirc;</p>
<p>Tune b&ucirc; sal&ecirc;n ber&ecirc;</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; Ferzendey&ecirc; me</p>
<h4>Avakir bo ko&ccedil;er&ecirc;</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ko&ccedil;ere malya w&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Bi temen ş&ecirc;st sal&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Nan &ucirc; dew dide wana</p>
<p>Ku derbasbin r&ecirc;w&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em zara hatne geşt&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dileyzin li v&ecirc; deşt&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nim&ecirc;j bikin durust bin</p>
<p>Ku h&ucirc;n herin bih&ucirc;şt&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hem&icirc; yanzdeh halik in</p>
<p>Bi mirişk&ucirc; berxik in</p>
<p>Bi pez &ucirc; qaz &ucirc; hesp in</p>
<p>L&ecirc; b&ecirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;lek golik in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Halik di erd&ecirc; da ne</p>
<p>Q&ucirc;ntara &ccedil;iy&ecirc; da ne</p>
<p>El&ecirc; din &ccedil;&ucirc;ne jor&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ev li v&ecirc; j&ecirc;r&ecirc; mane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mamost&ecirc; jin xwe berda</p>
<p>Li van rasta van erda</p>
<p>Veleziyan raneb&ucirc;n</p>
<p>Ferzende hat bi serda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li wana kire lanet</p>
<p>Li ber jin&ecirc; Kurda ket</p>
<p>Got jin&ecirc; me bi şerm in</p>
<p>Bi x&icirc;ret &ucirc; bi &icirc;ffet</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji Xirbe hatye erkan</p>
<p>Li vira b&ucirc;ye şivan</p>
<p>Gava ez hatim &ecirc;l&ecirc;</p>
<p>N&icirc;vro b&ucirc; w&icirc; dixwar nan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hatime v&icirc; zozan&icirc;</p>
<p>Ez &ccedil;&ucirc;me li ser kan&icirc;</p>
<p>Min destn&icirc;meja xwe girt</p>
<p>Ez &ccedil;&ucirc;me nava xan&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min nim&ecirc;ja n&icirc;vro kir</p>
<p>Ji Xweda ra lava kir</p>
<p>Rihmet li miry&ecirc; w&icirc; be</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; ev &ecirc;la ava kir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rihmet li d&ecirc;y&ucirc; bava</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; vira kirye ava</p>
<p>Li Hec&icirc; Ferzende be</p>
<p>Li gund&ecirc; Kurdzorava</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li k&ecirc;leka v&ecirc; r&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>R&ecirc;ya gund&ecirc; k&ecirc;ş&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Newala ku dikişe</p>
<p>&Ccedil;em&ecirc; Elbihar&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mal&ucirc; milk y&ecirc; Xwedan e</p>
<p>&Icirc;nsan li vir m&ecirc;van e</p>
<p>Li gund e li zozan e</p>
<p>Her dem bi &icirc;mt&icirc;han e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n birane h&ucirc;n kek in</p>
<p>Evana ji b&icirc;r nekin</p>
<p>&Icirc;nsan bin qenc&icirc; bikin</p>
<p>Mal &ucirc; milka z&ecirc;de kin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Z&ecirc;de bikin bi helal</p>
<p>Bibin meriv&ecirc;n delal</p>
<p>Serbilind bin her dem&icirc;</p>
<p>T&ecirc;r bixwin av&ecirc; zelal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Vexw&ucirc;n h&ucirc;n bikin şukr&ecirc;</p>
<p>Jib&icirc;r nekin fam kin fikr&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ne nankor bi wefa bin</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; ra bikin zikr&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zikir xweş e dewa ye</p>
<p>Ji bo qelba ş&icirc;fa ye</p>
<p>Xaniy&ecirc; meriv t&ecirc;da</p>
<p>Bi w&icirc; dibe ava ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew taet e nim&ecirc;j e</p>
<p>Bernede nebe g&ecirc;j e</p>
<p>Manew&icirc; paqij dike</p>
<p>Nah&ecirc;le tu qir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu heq&ecirc; w&ecirc; rind bid&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xweş helal bike ked&ecirc;</p>
<p>T&ecirc; qezenck&icirc; l&rsquo;axret&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; li Amed&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>MINNET</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nan&ecirc; xwe dixwim bi av&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nakş&icirc;nim minneta bav&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi dest&ecirc; xwe vedim b&icirc;r&ecirc;</p>
<h4>Avdim xiyar gul &ucirc; s&icirc;r&ecirc;</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tedaş&ecirc; bav&ecirc; xwe rar&icirc;</p>
<p>Ceyrana şebek&ecirc; birr&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez li vira mame b&ecirc; av</p>
<p>Erd&ecirc; dikolim gav bi gav</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Av&ecirc;n gundiyan tev hene</p>
<p>Ji ser&ecirc; wana z&ecirc;de ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me mala xwe li vir dan&icirc;</p>
<p>Em mane b&ecirc; av &ucirc; kan&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me &ccedil;endikek bostan av&ecirc;t</p>
<p>Em b&ucirc;n agir em b&ucirc;ne p&ecirc;t</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Her k&ecirc;s&icirc; av li me birr&icirc;</p>
<p>Dora me b&ucirc; kelem dirr&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Al&icirc; nekir m&ecirc;ro xorto</p>
<p>Av berneda mala p&ucirc;rto</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şemsedd&icirc;n cam&ecirc;r&icirc; dikir</p>
<p>L&ecirc; ava w&icirc; t&ecirc;r&ecirc; nekir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min ber der&icirc; b&icirc;r&ecirc; kola</p>
<p>Bi tevr&ecirc; hesin &ucirc; pola</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tevr&ecirc; min&ecirc; erd&ecirc; gezke</p>
<p>Av&ecirc; der&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; hezke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dalgi&ccedil;eke pi&ccedil;&ucirc;k t&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Nava b&icirc;r&ecirc; da dat&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>J&ecirc; derdixim aveke rind</p>
<p>Nakş&icirc;nim minneta tu gund</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta xelqa gundiya</p>
<p>Diş&icirc;nime ser&ecirc; &ccedil;iya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&ecirc; niha qenciy&ecirc; bike</p>
<p>Sub&ecirc; li te minnet dike</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; dost&ecirc; menfeet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xeyde her roj her seet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mesela av&ecirc; dir&ecirc;j e</p>
<p>Ziman nikare bib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em werin mijarek din&ecirc;</p>
<p>Hinek guh&ecirc; xwe bidin&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez &ucirc; N&ucirc;redd&icirc;ne c&icirc;nar</p>
<p>Li payton&ecirc; b&ucirc;ne siwar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo tend&ucirc;r&ecirc; b&icirc;nin xwel&icirc;</p>
<p>Bip&ecirc;jin nan &ccedil;&ecirc;kin qel&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&ecirc;s&icirc; ji me ra l&ecirc; nekir</p>
<p>Wan tend&ucirc;ra me &ccedil;&ecirc;nekir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bona nem&icirc;nim serbir&icirc;</p>
<p>Min tend&ucirc;reke n&ucirc; kir&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min doşka tend&ucirc;r&ecirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;kir</p>
<p>D&icirc;war dan&icirc; xwel&icirc; l&ecirc;kir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ten&ecirc; mame b&ecirc; xebatkar</p>
<p>Tiliya min b&ucirc; bir&icirc;ndar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi ten&ecirc; dikim xebat&ecirc;</p>
<p>L&ecirc; ez nakş&icirc;nim minnet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta xwuşk &ucirc; ya bir&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dih&ecirc;lim li ser&ecirc; pir&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta delala day&ecirc;</p>
<p>Weke kay&ecirc; didim bay&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta hevala xwuşk&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dav&ecirc;jime ber mir&icirc;şk&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta jin &ucirc; ya m&ecirc;ra</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; bav&ecirc;jim bi b&ecirc;ra</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta p&icirc;r&ecirc; &ucirc; kal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Dav&ecirc;jime pişta mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta met&ecirc; pismam&ecirc;</p>
<p>Diş&icirc;nime erd&ecirc; Şam&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta xatiy&ucirc; ap&ecirc;</p>
<p>Gir&ecirc;didim ez bi kap&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta xas&icirc; y&ucirc; xez&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Naynim n&ecirc;z&icirc;k dih&ecirc;lim d&ucirc;r</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Minneta balt&ucirc;z &ucirc; b&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>Diş&icirc;nime nava s&ucirc;k&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew k&icirc; dibe bila bibe</p>
<p>Ji dil be bona Xwed&ecirc; be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>X&ecirc;ra xwe bav&ecirc;je ber&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc; d&icirc;sa rojek der&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nizan be mas&icirc; &ucirc; baliq</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc; winda nake Xaliq</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bigerin bi niyeta qenc</p>
<p>Li bih&ucirc;şt&ecirc; h&ucirc;n dibin genc</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Her Xweda &ccedil;&ecirc;tir dizane</p>
<p>Ew serraf&ecirc; ser qelbane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>EMMAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Deşt&ucirc; &ccedil;iya digerim</p>
<p>Ez b&ecirc; bask im b&ecirc; per im</p>
<p>Pere pol&ecirc; min tune</p>
<h4>Ku bi ereb&ecirc; herim</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Emman eman eman</p>
<p>Dem b&ucirc;ye axirzeman</p>
<p>Emman eman eman</p>
<p>Ji f&icirc;tna axirzeman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di&ccedil;im T&icirc;ll&ecirc; j&rsquo;Zorava</p>
<p>Derbasb&ucirc;m j&rsquo;m&ecirc;rg&ucirc; ava</p>
<p>H&ecirc; xort im li ser xwe me</p>
<p>Xweda mala te ava</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ser&ecirc; sib&ecirc; ye sar e</p>
<p>Pale h&ecirc; nakin kare</p>
<p>Hav&icirc;n e palet&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Pale b&ucirc;ne xeware</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nakevim nav zeviya</p>
<p>R&ucirc;nan&ecirc;m l&rsquo;ber deviya</p>
<p>R&ecirc;ya min d&ucirc;r dir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Naseknim li ber siya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li xwe dikim ş&icirc;ret&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bo hilnedim minnet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ji pars&ecirc; neraz&icirc;me</p>
<p>Ya xelq&ecirc; ya dewlet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li &ccedil;iya li ber &ccedil;eman</p>
<p>Diq&icirc;rim dikim eman</p>
<p>Xweda me bipar&ecirc;ze</p>
<p>Ji f&icirc;tna axirzeman</p>

<h1>M&Ecirc;VAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em&icirc;n xelq&ecirc; Kerboran&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez an&icirc;m dan&icirc;m Tetwan&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ew Ferhan Nazim Ebdullah</p>
<p>Tev&ecirc; Xal&ucirc;q &ccedil;&ucirc;ne Wan&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira Ebdurrehman an&icirc;</p>
<p>Li bajar&ecirc; M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; dan&icirc;</p>
<p>Bir&ecirc;ketin &ecirc;var&ecirc; &ccedil;&ucirc;n</p>
<h4>Nesekin&icirc;n bi m&ecirc;van&icirc;</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji M&ecirc;rd&icirc;n&ecirc; hatin vira</p>
<p>Derbasb&ucirc;n ji av &ucirc; pira</p>
<p>Li mala me nan nexwarin</p>
<p>Ten&ecirc; silav birin b&rsquo;xwera</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo kek Se&icirc;d Ebdulqadir</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; heq ji wan dibe sadir</p>
<p>Ew li M&ecirc;rd&icirc;n&ecirc; bi kar in</p>
<p>Min li M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; vegirt &ccedil;adir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em hilkişyan Kela M&ucirc;ş&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ay vexwar bi &icirc;skan ş&ucirc;ş&ecirc;</p>
<p>Em m&ecirc;rb&ucirc;n me M&ucirc;ş s&ecirc;yr dikir</p>
<p>Pirek mab&ucirc;n l&rsquo;ber derg&ucirc;ş&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew heval&ecirc;n pir delal in</p>
<p>Biaqil in bi kemal in</p>
<p>Meriv&ecirc; hezkirin&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>M&icirc;na bira kek &ucirc; xal in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min &lsquo;evdalo ez reben&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li Tetwan&ecirc; mam bi ten&ecirc;</p>
<p>Otob&ecirc;sa Wan&ecirc; siwar b&ucirc;m</p>
<p>&Ccedil;&ucirc;m M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; ne&ccedil;&ucirc;m Eden&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ereb&ecirc; da me r&ecirc;w&icirc; me</p>
<p>B&ecirc; bil&ecirc;t im wek s&ecirc;w&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Pere pol&ecirc; min nemaye</p>
<p>N&icirc;vro ye ez pir bir&ccedil;&icirc; me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li hember&ecirc; min Nemr&ucirc;t e</p>
<p>B&ecirc; dar e &ccedil;iyak&icirc; r&ucirc;t e</p>
<p>Ciy&ecirc; xwe da sekiniye</p>
<p>Ne hewcey&ecirc; nan &ucirc; q&ucirc;te</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; min bigh&icirc;ne mal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Herim hewara delal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bila xwarinek&ecirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;ke</p>
<p>Spas bikim j&rsquo;bo heval&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>LI TETWAN&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rojek &ccedil;&ucirc;me Tetwan&ecirc;</p>
<p>K&ecirc;leka Gola Wan&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ka ew Bed&icirc;uzzeman</p>
<p>Medresa Zehra kan&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez geriyam li taxa</p>
<p>Ku herime qonaxa</p>
<p>Şevek&ecirc; b&ucirc;me m&ecirc;van</p>
<p>Mala &Icirc;sma&icirc;l axa</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ber av ber &ccedil;em di&ccedil;&ucirc;m&ecirc;</p>
<p>Neketim nava q&ucirc;m&ecirc;</p>
<p>Li Tetwan m&ecirc;van b&ucirc;m&ecirc;</p>
<p>Mala Sma&icirc;l&ecirc; F&ucirc;m&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zav&ecirc; Kek Şemsed&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Qus&ucirc;r j&ecirc;ra tun&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ji Lic&ecirc; Amed&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Li Tetwan&ecirc; dim&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Felaket e ev esra</p>
<p>Xw&icirc;n dir&ecirc;je li Besra</p>
<p>Birazy&ecirc; şeh&icirc;dan in</p>
<p>Xwuşka Esma &ucirc; Esra</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şeh&icirc;d Mele Izzedd&icirc;n</p>
<p>Heyran dib&ucirc; k&ecirc; bib&icirc;n</p>
<p>Kurdek heyf &ucirc; h&ecirc;ja b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; min da pir ş&ecirc;r&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>P&ecirc;nc bir&ecirc; şeh&icirc;d hene</p>
<p>Yek ji yek&icirc; z&ecirc;de ne</p>
<p>&lsquo;El&icirc; Osman Şemsedd&icirc;n</p>
<p>Yek Ces&icirc;m yek Em&icirc;n e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Meriv&ecirc; pir delal in</p>
<p>Bi başa ra heval in</p>
<p>Ji gund&ecirc; Panos&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Maq&ucirc;lin ş&icirc;r helal in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zav&ecirc; wan &Icirc;sma&icirc;l e</p>
<p>Nizane bike h&icirc;le</p>
<p>B&ucirc;ye b&ucirc;k xwuşka Esma</p>
<p>Bi hev b&ucirc;ne qa&icirc;le</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew miraz&ecirc; xwe şa bin</p>
<p>Li ser r&ecirc;ya Seyda bin</p>
<p>Wek Seyday&ecirc; Izzedd&icirc;n</p>
<p>Bi x&icirc;ret bi wefa bin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me ji Kop&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nikarim hildim top&ecirc;</p>
<p>D&icirc;sa doz&ecirc; bernadim</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; bajom v&ecirc; şop&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nizamedd&icirc;n e Seyda</p>
<p>W&icirc; şikandiye qeyda</p>
<p>Ketye nava r&ecirc;zana</p>
<p>&Icirc;lmek xweş kirye peyda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew &Icirc;sma&icirc;l c&icirc;nar in</p>
<p>Bi xebat in bi kar in</p>
<p>Ji w&ecirc; n&ucirc;ra Quran&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ne mehr&ucirc;m in bi par in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mal&ecirc; wan bibe ava</p>
<p>Kur&ecirc; wan bibin zava</p>
<p>Mala min li M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Li gund&ecirc; Kurdzorava</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez &Icirc;hsan N&ucirc;r&icirc; Paşa</p>
<p>Digerin deşt&ucirc; kaşa</p>
<p>Xweda me islah bike</p>
<p>T&ecirc;xe heval&ecirc; başa</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Neke heval&ecirc; p&icirc;sa</p>
<p>B&ecirc; şerma b&ecirc; nam&ucirc;sa</p>
<p>Ji r&ecirc;ya heq dernexe</p>
<p>R&ecirc;ya M&ucirc;hemmed &Icirc;sa</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zeman axir zemane</p>
<p>&Icirc;sa t&ecirc; j&rsquo;as&icirc;mane</p>
<p>P&ecirc;xember&ecirc; Xweda ye</p>
<p>Me p&ecirc; anye &icirc;mane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zore f&icirc;tneya deccal</p>
<p>Nehişt qud&ucirc;m&ucirc; mecal</p>
<p>Qaşo em m&ecirc;r&ecirc; xas b&ucirc;n</p>
<p>Kur&ecirc; w&icirc; Rostem&ecirc; Zal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Melay&ecirc; mey&ecirc; menş&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Li ber deccal kişand ş&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Ropo ew av&ecirc;t hevs&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nava wan z&icirc;ndan&ecirc;n k&ucirc;r</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>WELAT<br><br><br></h1>
<p>Ax welat ax Welat</p>
<p>Bi Bil&icirc;s bi Xelat</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc;m li r&ecirc; qerim&icirc;</p>
<p>Azadiya te nehat</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku&ccedil;ik, gur, rov&icirc;, hir&ccedil;e</p>
<p>Te kirine &ccedil;ar per&ccedil;e</p>
<p>Ketine ser te dixwin</p>
<p>Dev&ecirc; wan mir&ccedil;e mir&ccedil;e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi Mehabad bi Wan&icirc;</p>
<p>Bi Am&icirc;d bi Herran&icirc;</p>
<p>Bajar&ecirc; te gelek in</p>
<p>Qamişlo Sil&ecirc;man&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dijmin wek&icirc; beraz in</p>
<p>Ew x&ecirc;ra me naxwazin</p>
<p>Wa em neyar&ecirc; hev in</p>
<p>Ji k&ecirc; em bikin gazin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pirr&icirc; em &ccedil;avnebar in</p>
<p>Ji hevra dirr &ucirc; har in</p>
<p>Em rihm&ecirc; li hev nakin</p>
<p>Ji dil wek işkedar in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ucirc;me &lsquo;evdal&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez mame li ser&ecirc; r&ecirc;</p>
<p>Min ji erd&ecirc; ranakin</p>
<p>L&ecirc; p&ecirc;pes dikin k&ecirc; t&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ketim bext&ecirc; &ccedil;er&ccedil;iya</p>
<p>Zik t&ecirc;r&ecirc; &ccedil;av bir&ccedil;iya</p>
<p>Ku min ji erd&ecirc; rakin</p>
<p>Bibine li ser &ccedil;iya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iyay&ecirc; tey&icirc; Agir&icirc;</p>
<p>R&ucirc;niştiye digir&icirc;</p>
<p>Nav welat&ecirc; xelq&ecirc; da</p>
<p>Tu d&icirc;l &icirc; tu h&ecirc;s&icirc;r &icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu welat&ecirc; Kurdan &icirc;</p>
<p>Ciy&ecirc; kul &ucirc; derdan &icirc;</p>
<p>H&ecirc;s&icirc;r&ecirc; xay&icirc;nan &icirc;</p>
<p>Berdesty&ecirc; nemerdan &icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dora te misilman in</p>
<p>Misilman&ecirc; nezan in</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av nebar&ecirc; Kurdan in</p>
<p>Xulam&ecirc; gawiran in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ewlad&ecirc; te s&ecirc;w&icirc; ne</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ar birane c&ecirc;w&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Xelq&ecirc; keda wan xwarye</p>
<p>Loma &icirc;ro bir&ccedil;&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev welat Kurdistan e</p>
<p>War&ecirc; herd Se&icirc;da ne</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; Ş&ecirc;x Ehmed&ecirc; Xan&icirc;</p>
<p>Ciy&ecirc; Feqy&ecirc; Teyran e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Serhed&ecirc; te zozan e</p>
<p>Bak&ucirc;r&ecirc; te Botan e</p>
<p>Baş&ucirc;r&ecirc; te Soran e</p>
<p>Navenda te Xerzan e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>ZAROK&Ecirc;N FIL&Icirc;ST&Icirc;N</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zarok&ecirc;n xelq&ecirc; Filist&icirc;n</p>
<p>B&ucirc;ne heval&ecirc; rihist&icirc;n</p>
<p>Ji ber w&ecirc; zilma Cih&ucirc;yan</p>
<p>Nema ji wan ra ley&icirc;st&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>L&icirc;stika wan bi kevir e</p>
<p>Dijmin&ecirc; wana gawir e</p>
<p>Bi tang &ucirc; top &ucirc; roketa</p>
<p>Li wana dike agire</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kevir dav&ecirc;j&icirc;n bi desta</p>
<p>Li ser r&ecirc;ya li wan besta</p>
<p>Gule li ser wan dibare</p>
<p>Ew r&ucirc;nan&ecirc;n wek me mesta</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Herkes s&ecirc;yra wana dike</p>
<p>Bo neb&icirc;ne &ccedil;ava digre</p>
<p>Ew dimrin b&ecirc; mal dim&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Dinya dib&ecirc; bila bimre</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dayk&ecirc; wan herro digir&icirc;n</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; wan lorandin &ucirc; ş&icirc;n</p>
<p>&Icirc;sra&icirc;l m&ecirc;r &ucirc; zar kuştin</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; wana b&ucirc;ye bir&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Borre borra &Icirc;sra&icirc;l e</p>
<p>Li feq&icirc;ra dike h&icirc;le</p>
<p>Rihetiy&ecirc; nade wana</p>
<p>Para wan h&icirc;ştiye &ccedil;&icirc;le</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>&Icirc;RAQ</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Way&ecirc; way&ecirc; li min way&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Icirc;raq dişewite day&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kuffar&ecirc; agir berday&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kesek hewara wan nay&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Heywax li min heywax li min</p>
<p>Gelo y&ecirc; &ccedil;abe hal&ecirc; min</p>
<p>Per&icirc;şane welat&ecirc; min</p>
<p>Tiştek nay&ecirc; ji dest&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zare zara zarokane</p>
<p>Herro kuştine talane</p>
<p>Ew xirab dikin malane</p>
<p>Dikujin p&icirc;r &ucirc; kalane</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Cinaze dikevin erda</p>
<p>Xw&icirc;na sor dikişe berda</p>
<p>Kesek tune were serda</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc;m war&ecirc; kul &ucirc; derda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>NEMR&Ucirc;DE BIL&Icirc;SE</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Erd &ucirc; ezman zewic&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Ewlad him tek him c&ecirc;w&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Erd &ucirc; ezman di nav xwe da</p>
<p>Pir huneran dihew&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h4>Erd p&icirc;reke ezman m&ecirc;r e</h4>
<p>Ser da dibar&icirc;ne x&ecirc;re</p>
<p>Erd ber&ecirc; xwe hevraz dike</p>
<p>Ezman dinh&ecirc;re l&rsquo;berj&ecirc;re</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iya ewtad &ccedil;iya st&ucirc;n in</p>
<p>Wek&icirc; &ccedil;adir m&icirc;na kon in</p>
<p>Pir xez&icirc;na xwey&icirc; dikin</p>
<p>Embara erzaq &ucirc; non in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew ne rihmetiy&ecirc; Nemr&ucirc;t</p>
<p>Xwe j&rsquo;edvara kirib&ucirc; p&ucirc;t</p>
<p>Nav&ecirc; xwe daye du &ccedil;iya</p>
<p>Ew li dojeh&icirc; dixwe q&ucirc;t</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li v&ecirc; gol&ecirc; dikim seyran</p>
<p>Ez ec&ecirc;b mam b&ucirc;me heyran</p>
<p>Ku min ev ava zelal d&icirc;t</p>
<p>Hat bira min Feqy&ecirc; Teyran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev Nemr&ucirc;d&ecirc; Bil&icirc;s&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Ber Tetwan&ecirc; hinda r&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Goleke xweş li ser heye</p>
<p>Hav&icirc;n&ecirc; ciy&ecirc; geşt&ecirc; ye</p>

<h1>ŞAKIR</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lawo lawo lawo Şakir</p>
<p>Te &icirc;ro berx&ecirc; xwe &ccedil;akir</p>
<p>Meha Receb roja &icirc;n&ecirc;</p>
<p>Te mala xwe ji vir barkir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek digir&icirc;n dib&ecirc;n bira</p>
<p>Te em xistin nav agira</p>
<p>Ya ku hatye ser&ecirc; me da</p>
<p>Ney&ecirc; ser&ecirc; tu kevira</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Şakir kete baraj&ecirc; da</p>
<p>Xeniq&icirc; di v&icirc;raj&ecirc; da</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; meriv diperite</p>
<h4>Di nava qaje qaj&ecirc; da</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Te agir xist mala bav&ecirc;</p>
<p>Tu b&ucirc;y&ecirc; şeh&icirc;d&ecirc; av&ecirc;</p>
<p>Day&icirc;ka te pir digir&icirc;</p>
<p>Dilor&icirc;ne dide nav&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ibkim mirin emr&ecirc; Xweda</p>
<p>T&ecirc; bi bela ge bi qeda</p>
<p>Zar&ucirc; mal y&ecirc; kes&icirc; n&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Xweda emanet da me da</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Emr&ecirc; Xweda li ser &ccedil;ava</p>
<p>Ha bi roja ha bi şeva</p>
<p>Roja k&ecirc; were y&ecirc; bimre</p>
<p>Dor&ecirc; w&ecirc; were me teva</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pez dibirrim bi hevr&icirc;ng&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nizam ez&ecirc; bimrim k&icirc;ng&ecirc;</p>
<p>Heta sax be dewsa te da</p>
<p>X&icirc;yas di&ccedil;e ber dir&ucirc;ng&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ya Reb tu me bike şakir</p>
<p>Ziman&ecirc; me bike zakir</p>
<p>Seb xatir&ecirc; w&icirc; Şakir&icirc;</p>
<p>Ku te ew ji nav me rakir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu li w&icirc; bike rehmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bike teyrik&ecirc; cennet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Sebr&ecirc; bide d&ecirc; bav&ecirc; w&icirc;</p>
<p>Heta roja qiyamet&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Paşda na&ccedil;e ecel were</p>
<p>Hezk&icirc; bide milyar pere</p>
<p>K&ecirc; ji mirin&ecirc; ders negre</p>
<p>Yan b&ecirc;hişe yan j&icirc; ker e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>DA&Icirc;MA BIB&Ecirc;JE</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu dixwaz&icirc; xilas b&icirc;</p>
<p>Berj&ecirc;r neb&icirc; hevraz b&icirc;</p>
<p>Dil &ucirc; can bi awaz b&icirc;</p>
<p>Da&icirc;ma tu bib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>La &icirc;lahe &Icirc;llellah</p>
<p>Muhemmed Res&ucirc;l&ucirc;llah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bona tu şaş neb&icirc;</p>
<p>Li d&ucirc; &lsquo;evda kaş neb&icirc;</p>
<p>Dinyay&ecirc; da faş neb&icirc;</p>
<p>Da&icirc;ma tu bib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>La &icirc;lahe &Icirc;llellah</p>
<p>Muhemmed Res&ucirc;l&ucirc;llah</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>La &icirc;lahe &Icirc;llellah</p>
<p>Muhemmed Res&ucirc;l&ucirc;llah</p>

<p>Melek dora te hebe</p>

<p>Muhemmed Res&ucirc;l&ucirc;llah</p>

<h1>EMAN EMAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Eman eman eman eman eman eman eman ez&ecirc; li deşta M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; dinh&ecirc;rim ez ser&ecirc; w&ecirc;</p>
<p>dib&icirc;nim &ccedil;av&ecirc; min dawya w&ecirc; nab&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>Dengb&ecirc;jek dist&icirc;re dib&ecirc;j&ecirc; dinya fan&icirc; ye derew&icirc;n e.</p>
<p>Welleh ez j&icirc; dizanim dinya fan&icirc; ji bav&ecirc; me Adem Siltan Sil&ecirc;man Muhemmed</p>
<p>Mistefa bav&ecirc; Fatimay&ecirc; ra nema, ji kes&icirc; bav&ecirc; kes&icirc; ra nam&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>Mirin ji hem&ucirc; kes&icirc; ra yek e firqa feq&icirc;r &ucirc; zeng&icirc;na, şivan &ucirc; siltana, zar &ucirc; mezina jin &ucirc;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;ra tin&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>Rica &ucirc; gazina j&icirc; we dikim di s&ecirc; roj&ecirc; jiyana dinyay&ecirc; da kar &ucirc; xebata xwe rind bikin, ji herama xwe d&ucirc;r bigrin maf&ecirc; kes&icirc; li xwe neh&ecirc;lin bila derd &ucirc; kul di kul di dil&ecirc; we da nem&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>Eman eman eman eman eman ji şerr&ecirc; nefs&ecirc; bela jinan ji fitna axirzeman.</p>
<p>Eman eman eman eman eman Eman ez&ecirc; li Gola Wan&ecirc; m&ecirc;ze dikim reng&ecirc; ava w&ecirc; h&ecirc;ş&icirc;n e.</p>
<p>Em ji M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; di&ccedil;in Wan&ecirc; heval&ecirc; min kek&ecirc; Sel&icirc;m mamoste Muhemmed, &Icirc;brah&icirc;m&ecirc;</p>
<p>Kurmanc, Salih&ecirc; kinik&ecirc; zar ş&ecirc;r&icirc;n e.</p>
<p>Dinya &icirc;mt&icirc;han e em j&icirc; di&ccedil;in &icirc;mt&icirc;han&ecirc; ji bon&ecirc; xebata me hindike t&ecirc;r&ecirc; n&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>H&ecirc;viya me ma li duay&ecirc; heval &ucirc; hogira dost&ecirc; ji dil, duay&ecirc; qencan, li jor cem Rebb&ecirc;</p>
<p>Alem&ecirc; Reh&icirc;m &ucirc; Rehman Hennan&ecirc; Mennan wes&icirc;la me Fexr&ecirc; Alem ronya &ccedil;ava Siltan&ecirc; lewlak şah&ecirc; erd &ucirc; ezm&ecirc;n e.</p>
<p>Li gerd&ucirc;n&ecirc; em b&ecirc;kes in b&ecirc;&ccedil;are ne maf&ecirc; me qedexe ye belk&icirc; Xweda Hezret&icirc; Xizir li hewara me biş&icirc;ne.</p>
<p>Eman eman eman eman eman ji şerr&ecirc; nefs&ecirc; bela jinan ji fitna axirzeman.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>NEXAPE</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ey biray&ecirc; min&ecirc; Teyy&icirc;b</p>
<p>Faniyan da nebe qey&icirc;b</p>
<p>Sebir bike m&icirc;na Eyy&ucirc;b</p>
<h4>Bigh&ecirc;je Ellamul Xuy&ucirc;b</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi faniyan ve nem&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Tu nexape nebe d&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Dil &ucirc; aqil&ecirc; xwe b&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Xweday&ecirc; Baq&icirc; bib&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Were bi jina nexape</p>
<p>Xwe nexe wer&icirc;s &ucirc; kape</p>
<p>Liva hilde berde sape</p>
<p>Bo av&ecirc; nebe b&ecirc; pape</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Jin m&icirc;nan&icirc; dinyay&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Carna d&ecirc;l in m&icirc;na s&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Carna başin wek&icirc; d&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Fan&icirc;ne &lsquo;evd&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu b&ecirc;n bike m&icirc;na gula</p>
<p>Nexape bi &ccedil;av &ucirc; kila</p>
<p>Mas&icirc;va nexe nav dila</p>
<p>Pir nekş&icirc;ne derd &ucirc; kula</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Icirc;mt&icirc;hana Mecn&ucirc;n Leyla</p>
<p>Li ser&ecirc; w&icirc; bib&ucirc; bela</p>
<p>Ber &ccedil;av&ecirc; w&icirc; bib&ucirc; kela</p>
<p>L&ecirc; w&icirc; berda gih&icirc;şt Mewla</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hinek&icirc; k&ucirc;r bih&ecirc;zire</p>
<p>Ji Mecn&ucirc;n ders&ecirc; bigire</p>
<p>Birj&icirc;ne ji &ccedil;av h&ecirc;sir e</p>
<p>Tobeke paş&ecirc; bimire</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Faniyan da winda nebe</p>
<p>Bila haya te j&rsquo;te hebe</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; ku hay ji xwe tune be</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc; daw&icirc; şepirze be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&ecirc;&ccedil;are me v&ecirc; dizanim</p>
<p>H&icirc;le dolaba nizanim</p>
<p>B&ecirc; zev&icirc; me b&ecirc; xozan im</p>
<p>Ne aşiq im helbestvan im</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>HESENKEYF</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hesenkeyfe</p>
<p>Şehrek heyf e</p>
<p>P&ecirc;n&ucirc;sa min</p>
<h4>Ş&ucirc;r &ucirc; seyf e</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez dinv&icirc;sim</p>
<p>B&rsquo;dil &ucirc; h&icirc;s im</p>
<p>Dest&ecirc; hozan</p>
<p>Radim&ucirc;sim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tevşo tevir</p>
<p>Hutik bivir</p>
<p>P&ecirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;dibe</p>
<p>Neqşa kevir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&icirc;roka vir</p>
<p>B&ucirc;ye nemir</p>
<p>Wan niv&icirc;sye</p>
<p>Li ser kevir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji kevire</p>
<p>Ders bigire</p>
<p>Bi wan b&ucirc;ye</p>
<p>Kel &ucirc; pire</p>

<h1>ŞIYAR&Icirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek&ecirc; ji me ra qise kir</p>
<p>Ew&icirc; beşera me vekir</p>
<p>Raman&ecirc;n w&icirc; pir delal b&ucirc;n</p>
<p>Şir&icirc;n b&ucirc;n m&icirc;nan&icirc; şekir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xweşe ku fikra bib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Di d&icirc;za dil da bip&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Wek&icirc; barana rehmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ser mihtaca da bir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek Hem&icirc;d ji Erxeniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Av vexwarye ji kaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Pi&ccedil;&ucirc;ka b&ecirc; av nah&ecirc;le</p>
<p>Ew baş dike şivaniy&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em hatine v&icirc; diyar&icirc;</p>
<p>Me d&icirc;t &ccedil;akiye şiyar&icirc;</p>
<p>Hezkirin &ccedil;iqas&icirc; rind e</p>
<p>&Ccedil;iqas qir&ecirc;je neyar&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Id&icirc; em b&ucirc;ne bajar&icirc;</p>
<p>Mij&ucirc;l dibin bi kubar&icirc;</p>
<p>Medeniyet t&ecirc; nava me</p>
<p>L&ecirc; hindik t&ecirc; par&icirc; par&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>W&icirc; got werin em bibin em</p>
<p>Hesp&ecirc; siwar bin l&ecirc;bixin gem</p>
<p>Wek&icirc; gel&ecirc;n p&ecirc;şda &ccedil;&ucirc;y&icirc;</p>
<p>Biherikin m&icirc;nan&icirc; &ccedil;em.</p>

<h1>DE LO LO</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu xel&icirc;f&ecirc; Ş&ecirc;x Se&icirc;d&ecirc; ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; delal ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; Palo</p>
<p>Te diajot r&ecirc;ya rasta p&ecirc;xembera r&ecirc;ya bav &ucirc; kalo</p>
<p>Heta sax bim li dinyay&ecirc; te jib&icirc;r nakim roj &ucirc; şeva lo meh &ucirc; salo</p>
<p>Te mal barkir ji vir &ccedil;&ucirc;y&icirc; em man h&ecirc;s&icirc;r &ucirc; &lsquo;evdalo</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo ez B&ecirc;&ccedil;are ez &lsquo;evdalo</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Belk&icirc; Xwed&ecirc; xirab bike mala kemo mala wan romiya</p>
<p>&Ccedil;awa bi dest&ecirc; ş&ecirc;x&ecirc;m girtin birin hinda pira li ser&ecirc; riya</p>
<p>Bi &icirc;şkence zilm&ucirc; teda ş&ecirc;x&ecirc;m kuştin wan hoviya</p>
<p>Ez dibecim ş&ecirc;r&ecirc; &ccedil;iya zar&ecirc; Rostem &icirc;ro b&ucirc;ne h&ecirc;s&icirc;r&ecirc; roviya</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo ez B&ecirc;&ccedil;are ez &lsquo;evdalo</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; min&ecirc; Mihme Em&icirc;n ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; M&ucirc;ş&ecirc; tu xelq&ecirc; Xaziya</p>
<p>Tu heval&ecirc; xelq&ecirc; feq&icirc;r xelq&ecirc; bindest me bir&ccedil;iy&ucirc; me teziya</p>
<p>Yec&ucirc;c mec&ucirc;c zar&ecirc; sufyan bo te b&ucirc;n mer lo b&ucirc;ne ziya</p>
<p>Mala te birin roava tev&ecirc; zara jin &ucirc; kala xwuşk &ucirc; bira biraziya</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo de lo lo lo lo li lo lo,</p>
<p>De lo lo lo lo lo lo lo ez B&ecirc;&ccedil;are ez &lsquo;evdalo</p>

<h1>Ş&Ecirc;X&Ecirc; XAZİYA</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Quwet&ecirc; bide paz&ucirc;ya</p>
<p>Ji bona ş&ecirc;x&ecirc; xaziya</p>
<p>Nesekine xebat bike</p>
<p>Bese tu bike naziya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xay&icirc;na ew şeh&icirc;d kirin</p>
<p>Mala w&icirc; ji vir bar kirin</p>
<p>Ş&ecirc;x &ucirc; melay&ecirc; bi x&icirc;ret</p>
<p>Wan ji nava me rakirin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em wek peza gura xwar&icirc;</p>
<p>Ji hev kirin ker&icirc; ker&icirc;</p>
<p>Em man b&ecirc;&ccedil;are belengaz</p>
<p>Wana em h&icirc;ştin b&ecirc; ser&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez digerim der&icirc; b&rsquo;der&icirc;</p>
<p>Bi nama l&ecirc; dixim ser&icirc;</p>
<p>Belk&icirc; şivan hişyar bibin</p>
<p>B&ecirc; xwey&icirc; nem&icirc;ne ker&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pişt&icirc; ş&ecirc;x Muhemmed Em&icirc;n</p>
<p>Ez &ccedil;i dikim li ser zem&icirc;n</p>
<p>R&ecirc; d&ucirc;re em&ecirc; j&icirc; herin</p>
<p>Zex&icirc;r&ecirc; bikine tem&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mele M&ucirc;sa Feqy&ecirc; Seyda</p>
<p>&Icirc;lmek&icirc; xweş kirye peyda</p>
<p>Bi &icirc;zna Xweday&ecirc; el&icirc;m</p>
<p>W&ecirc; b&icirc;şk&ecirc;ne bend &ucirc; qeyda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bend&ecirc; &icirc;rada me Kurda</p>
<p>Ketiye dest ulema da</p>
<p>Ku lime xwey&icirc; derkevin</p>
<p>Em digh&icirc;jin alema da</p>

<h1>HER&Ecirc; L&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Welat&ecirc; me serhede sare zivistane</p>
<p>Aqil &ucirc; hiş&ecirc; me qerisye bin&ecirc; berf&ecirc; da mane</p>
<p>Zuryeta Rostem&ecirc; Zal Silhed&icirc;n&ecirc; Eyy&ucirc;b&icirc; Bed&icirc;uzzeman Se&icirc;d&ecirc; Kurd&icirc; razane di xew da ne</p>
<p>Meriv ş&ecirc;r&ecirc; &ccedil;iya be h&ecirc;s&icirc;r&ecirc; h&ecirc;s&icirc;ra be girtiy&ecirc; roviya be derd&ecirc; hem &ucirc; derdane her&ecirc; l&ecirc;</p>
<p>De her&ecirc; l&ecirc; her&ecirc; l&ecirc; ez nizan&icirc;m ez&ecirc; kuda her&icirc;m derd&ucirc;, keder&ucirc;, keser&ecirc; mereq&ecirc; dil&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>bib&ecirc;jim k&ecirc; y&ucirc; k&ecirc;.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; &ccedil;&ucirc;me Batman&ecirc; Hesenk&ecirc;f&ecirc; Cizra Bota ciy&ecirc; Mem&ecirc; Alan e</p>
<p>Min nih&ecirc;r&icirc; li kelaya li kevira li pira li minara ne</p>
<p>Kevira hev hem&ecirc;zkirne ser&icirc; kutane hev ji bona belav nebin, nekevin erd&ecirc;, bim&icirc;nin li piyane</p>
<p>Gelo dil&ecirc; me j&rsquo;kevira kevirtir e, welat&ecirc; me bindest e kela &icirc;man&ecirc; hilşiya ye em &ccedil;ima şiyar nabin dest&ecirc; hev nagrin m&icirc;nan&icirc; ş&ecirc;ran&ucirc; m&ecirc;ra naqet&icirc;nin zinc&icirc;ra bi rast&icirc; ji hevra nabin birane</p>
<p>De her&ecirc; l&ecirc; her&ecirc; l&ecirc; ez nizan&icirc;m ez&ecirc; kuda her&icirc;m derd&ucirc; keder&ucirc;, keser&ecirc; mereq&ecirc; dil&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>bib&ecirc;jim k&ecirc; y&ucirc; k&ecirc;.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; ji M&ucirc;şa şewt&icirc; r&ecirc;ketim &ccedil;&ucirc;me Amed&ecirc; derd&ecirc; dil&ecirc; min girane</p>
<p>Kuffar&ecirc; mala me xirab kirye agit berda ye nawa dil&ecirc; misilmane</p>
<p>Qije qije &icirc;mana me dşewite alev &ucirc; p&ecirc;ta xwe g&icirc;handye as&icirc;mane</p>
<p>Ez&ecirc; &ccedil;&ucirc;me bajar&ecirc; S&ecirc;rt&ecirc; ser tirba Melle Xel&icirc;l d&ucirc;ra &ccedil;&ucirc;me Tilloy&ecirc; ser merqeda Feq&icirc;r&ucirc;llah bi dil&ecirc; şewt&icirc; &ccedil;av&ecirc; h&ecirc;s&icirc;r min dest&ecirc; xwe vekir ji Xaliq Rebb&ecirc; alem&ecirc; ra, belk&icirc; ji rihm&ucirc; kerema xwe baranek&ecirc; bibar&icirc;ne awek&ecirc; l&ecirc; ke, bitemr&icirc;ne v&icirc; agir&ecirc; hane her&ecirc; l&ecirc;.</p>
<p>De her&ecirc; l&ecirc; her&ecirc; l&ecirc; ez nizan&icirc;m ez&ecirc; kuda her&icirc;m derd&ucirc; keder&ucirc;, keser&ecirc; mereq&ecirc; dil&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>bib&ecirc;jim k&ecirc; y&ucirc; k&ecirc;.</p>

<h1>MIRIN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&icirc;ran&icirc;na mirin&ecirc; j&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; mirin&ecirc; jib&icirc;r ke d&icirc;n e</p>
<p>H&ecirc; ecel&ecirc; te nehatiye</p>
<p>Tu were tevd&icirc;r&ecirc; bib&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ecirc; z&ucirc;ye neb&ucirc;ye &ecirc;vare</p>
<p>D&ucirc; zivistan&ecirc; t&ecirc; bihare</p>
<p>Were bil&ecirc;tek&ecirc; bist&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Nem&icirc;ne dest vala b&ecirc; pare</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji mirin&ecirc; kes nabe xilas</p>
<p>Kefen rojek&ecirc; dibe kiras</p>
<p>C&ecirc;v &ucirc; b&ecirc;r&icirc;ka kefen tine</p>
<p>Mal &ucirc; milk tev dim&icirc;ne m&icirc;ras</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hesab&ecirc; mal &ucirc; milka heye</p>
<p>Milk z&ecirc;debe hesab z&ecirc;de ye</p>
<p>Mal&ecirc; heram hem&icirc; ezab e</p>
<p>Bela ser&ecirc; xweyiy&ecirc; xwe ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mirin m&icirc;na j&icirc;n&ecirc; jiyan e</p>
<p>Heyeta li wir heyewan e</p>
<p>Jiyana vir wek&icirc; xewnan e</p>
<p>J&icirc;na rast&icirc; li pişt qebran e</p>

<h1>HINEK XORT LI BATMAN&Ecirc;</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&ucirc;rad bira ye keke</p>
<p>Herro t&ucirc;ncik&ecirc; şeke</p>
<p>Bo zarokan &ucirc; xortan</p>
<h4>Der&icirc; paca tu veke</h4>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Biray&ecirc; delal B&icirc;lal</p>
<p>J&icirc;r bibe nebe &lsquo;evdal</p>
<p>Strana xweş bib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Bistir&ecirc; qet nebe lal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu wek B&icirc;lal&ecirc; Hebeş</p>
<p>M&icirc;na gula bibe geş</p>
<p>Dest ji n&ucirc;r&ecirc; bernede</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; dostan bike xweş</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo birako lo Yehya</p>
<p>Heta sola te mehya</p>
<p>Xebat&ecirc; bidom&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Here r&ecirc;ya Zekerya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi berxwedan be Yilmaz</p>
<p>Bo Xwed&ecirc; bike niyaz</p>
<p>M&icirc;na wan moz&ecirc; hingiv</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; xwe baş bike saz</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira Muhemmed Em&icirc;n</p>
<p>Hespek&icirc; bike tem&icirc;n</p>
<p>Bo xizmeta Quran&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bigere li ser zem&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo Y&ucirc;n&ucirc;so lo bira</p>
<p>Te nexwe masy&ecirc; behra</p>
<p>Bi nefsa xwe nexape</p>
<p>Bike qenciy&ucirc; x&ecirc;ra</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ednan&ecirc; qadastroy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Şor n&icirc;ne m&icirc;na xoy&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bi fed&icirc; ye bi şerm e</p>
<p>Ew hez dike ji şoy&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ş&ecirc;r&ecirc; panos&ecirc; Yuksel</p>
<p>M&icirc;na zinar wek&icirc; sel</p>
<p>Bi xebat e bi kar e</p>
<p>J&ecirc;hatiye ne tenbel</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Halis muhlistir Aşır</p>
<p>B&uuml;y&uuml;k y&uuml;kleri taşır</p>
<p>Her g&uuml;n b&uuml;t&uuml;n şerlerle</p>
<p>Nefis ile savaşır</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mem&ecirc; xortek&icirc; baş e</p>
<p>Xeberdana w&icirc; xweş e</p>
<p>R&ecirc;ber&ecirc; şakirdane</p>
<p>Ne mela ye b&ecirc; şaş e</p>

<h1>NEKIN ŞER</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Berfa nava gund heliya Xirabşer Xirabşer</p>

<h1>DERY&Ecirc; M&Ecirc;RD&Icirc;N</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di roja da duşem e</p>
<p>Zeman j&icirc; esir de me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li hember&ecirc; mine s&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Ew bilind bin&ecirc; w&ecirc; k&ucirc;r</p>

<p>Du sip&icirc; s&ecirc; reş yek gewr</p>

<p>Dib&icirc;nim ku b&ucirc;ye kal</p>

<p>Derna tem&icirc;r kirine</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Kesk dikin l&ecirc; b&ucirc;ne xar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li min dixe ev tava</p>
<p>Hindik ma here ava</p>

<p>Amed bajarek kevn e</p>
<p>D&icirc;roka w&ecirc; wek xewn e</p>

<h1>L&Ecirc; EMAN</h1><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min&ecirc; &ccedil;av&ecirc; xwe j&rsquo;xew&ecirc; vekir got ya Allah ya Xwed&ecirc; nim&ecirc;ja şeweq&ecirc; kir min nih&ecirc;r&icirc; wa sibe ye</p>
<p>Min perde da al&icirc; di pac&ecirc; m&ecirc;zekir li deşta Batman&ecirc; deştek pir fire ye</p>
<p>Ez rab&ucirc;m li dolm&icirc;ş&ecirc; siwar b&ucirc;m &ccedil;&ucirc;me Bismil&ecirc; du ra Amed&ecirc; paytext&ecirc; Kurdistan&ecirc; bajar&ecirc; bav &ucirc; kal&ecirc; me ye</p>
<p>Ez ji zar &ucirc; pi&ccedil;&ucirc;ka, xort &ucirc; ke&ccedil;a, m&ecirc;r &ucirc; jina, kal &ucirc; p&icirc;ra ra dib&ecirc;jim ji hev hezkin qedr&ecirc; hev bizan bin di s&ecirc; roj&ecirc; jiyana gerd&ucirc;n&ecirc; da y&ecirc; ku qedr&ecirc; hev nizan be, tevlihev be per&icirc;şan be, pir heyfe zehf yazixe şepirze ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mele Yuksel mel&ecirc; delal ji Panos&ecirc; hatye vira, dib&ecirc; gel&icirc; bira werin hewceya me b&rsquo;hev heye</p>
<p>Welat&ecirc; me serhede, xerzane, botane, sorane war&ecirc; Rostem&ecirc; Zal, Silhedd&icirc;n&ecirc; Eyy&ucirc;biy&ecirc; kalk&ecirc; me ye</p>
<p>Gel&ecirc; me oldar e, misilmane, x&icirc;reta &icirc;man&ecirc;, cam&ecirc;riy&ecirc;, welatperweriy&ecirc;, mirovahiy&ecirc; di dil&ecirc; wan da tije ye</p>
<p>Em ji bona d&icirc;n &ucirc; welat&ecirc; xwe x&icirc;ret bikin, r&ecirc;ya wan xweş m&ecirc;ra, cam&ecirc;ra bajon, m&icirc;na teyr&ecirc; bi du baska difire, bo dinya &ucirc; axret&ecirc; kar&ecirc; xwe z&ecirc;dekin sekna me zirar e b&ecirc; fayde ye.</p>

<h1>XWED&Ecirc; ALLAH HEWAR!</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&icirc;h&ecirc; didim b&rsquo;bizin&ecirc;</p>

<p>Rebb&icirc; yess&icirc;r!</p>
<p>Wela tuess&icirc;r!</p>
<p>Sehh&icirc;l eleyna!</p>
<p>B&icirc; fadl&icirc;ke</p>
<p>Ya Muyess&icirc;r! ALLAH!</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi şev&ecirc; televizyon</p>
<p>Bi roj&ecirc; dunyav&icirc;zyon</p>
<p>Nefis b&ucirc;ye şampiyon</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; Allah Hewar!</p>

<h1>KU DA HERIM</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>CES&Icirc;M DIB&Ecirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Ces&icirc;m dib&ecirc; Huseyn&ecirc; bira malik neşewityo de rabe, ser&ecirc; xwe rake, &ccedil;eva veke ji v&ecirc; xewa şir&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Pişt&icirc; şeh&icirc;db&ucirc;na Seyday&ecirc; Mele &Icirc;zzed&icirc;n li w&ecirc;rana Antalya wefat kirye Seyfedd&icirc;n&ecirc; N&ucirc;jdar&ecirc; heval&ecirc; Seyda ew xizmeta wane giranbiha ma h&ecirc;v&icirc;ya me &lsquo;evdala derd&ecirc; min girane hal&ecirc; min tin&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Ca tu rabe here cav&ecirc; bide Ra&icirc;f&ecirc; B&ecirc;&ccedil;are bav&ecirc; &Icirc;hsan N&ucirc;r&icirc; xelq&ecirc; Gely&ecirc; Z&icirc;lan bila kilamek&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;ke bilor&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bila m&ecirc;r&ecirc; tofan &ucirc; teşqela &lsquo;Evdilah&ecirc; &ccedil;evbelek tev&ecirc; &lsquo;eg&icirc;t&ecirc; xorta, ş&ecirc;x &ucirc; meşayixa, mezin &ucirc; r&ecirc;zana p&ecirc; bihes&icirc;ne</p>

<p>Ces&icirc;m dib&ecirc; Huseyn&ecirc; bira pay&icirc;ze ji kula dil&ecirc; min ra xweş pay&icirc;ze.</p>
<p>Derd&ecirc; min giran e keser&ecirc; min gelekin dil&ecirc; min bi kule x&icirc;ze x&icirc;ze.Xizmeta &icirc;man&ecirc;,doza Medresa Zehray&ecirc; di dil&ecirc; min da pir şir&icirc;n e zehf ez&icirc;ze.Weyla malik neşewityo ca tu rabe ,were x&icirc;ret&ecirc;,bixebite ji bona axret&ecirc;,mal&ucirc; milk&ecirc; dinya fan&icirc; ji meriv ra nam&icirc;ne ,zar&ucirc; z&ecirc;&ccedil; &ucirc; ke&ccedil; &ucirc; q&icirc;z e.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ces&icirc;m dib&ecirc; Huseyn&ecirc; bira &icirc;ro ji kula dil&ecirc; min ra sar e,seqem e,zivistan e.Berf bar&icirc;ye &ccedil;ar aliya ,li me girtye r&ecirc; &ucirc; p&ecirc; ji me ra nemaye ne m&ecirc;rg &ucirc; zev&icirc; ne erd&ecirc; reş ne bax e ne bostan e.Ca tu rabe malik neşewityo,hinek&icirc; xwe bişid&icirc;ne,&icirc;ro roja teng e,roja m&ecirc;ran e,ne roja xewara,tirsoneka lo ne roja sista ne.Ji bona xelq&ecirc; me p&ecirc;şkeve nesekine,xebat bike li mekteb &ucirc; dibistan e.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ces&icirc;m dib&ecirc; Huseyn&ecirc; bira d&icirc;sa ji kula dil&ecirc; min ra bihare xweş bihar e.Berf heliya,gul vedibin,m&ecirc;rg h&ecirc;ş&icirc;n b&ucirc;n m&icirc;na par e.Ca tu rabe malik neşewityo, bostan avde,l&ecirc; binh&ecirc;r e &icirc;ro ne roja sekn&ecirc; ye,xew xeflete pir zirar e. Em&ecirc; cot &ucirc; kotan&ecirc; xwe bikin,tova bireş&icirc;nin,belk&icirc; bax&ecirc; me j&icirc; &ccedil;&ecirc;be,Xweda y&ecirc; alem&ecirc; ji aly&ecirc; xwe da ji me ra biş&icirc;ne h&ecirc;v&icirc; y&ucirc; sitar &ucirc; hewar e.</p>

<p>Xwendin emrek&icirc; Xweda ye</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek&ecirc; h&ecirc;ja Mihme Sel&icirc;m</p>
<p>Mervek&icirc; k&ecirc;fxweş ,hel&icirc;m</p>
<p>Xweda jiyana we başke</p>
<p>Nede we da derd&ecirc;n el&icirc;m</p>

<h1>KEK&Ecirc;&nbsp; SID&Icirc;Q</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek&ecirc; Sid&icirc;q Şeyxanzade</p>

<p>Bi qudreta Rebb&ecirc; Qadir</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rab&ucirc; ji nava B&icirc;ngol &ecirc;</p>

<p>Rastiya R&icirc;sal&ecirc; kola</p>
<p>B&ecirc; xwed&icirc; neh&icirc;şt li &ccedil;ol&ecirc;</p>

<h1>KERM&Ecirc;Ş</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&icirc;sa li me b&ucirc; &ecirc;var</p>
<p>Kerm&ecirc;şan xw&icirc;na me xwar</p>
<p>W&ecirc; bixwin wek&icirc; her car</p>
<p>Ax ji derd&ecirc; kerm&ecirc;şan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew &ecirc;r&icirc;ş&icirc; me dikin</p>
<p>Em ji wan aciz dibin</p>
<p>Xw&icirc;n&ecirc; bi ser me dixin</p>
<p>Ax ji kula kerm&ecirc;şan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dora me tev bax&ccedil;e ne</p>
<p>Dar&ecirc;n h&ecirc;ş&icirc;n pir hene</p>
<p>Kerm&ecirc;ş&ecirc; wan z&ecirc;de ne</p>
<p>Ax ji jana kerm&ecirc;şan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ser me de q&ucirc;je q&ucirc;j in</p>
<p>Derz&icirc;y&ecirc;n wan pir t&ucirc;j in</p>
<p>Qul dikin m&icirc;na ş&ucirc;jin</p>
<p>Ax ji we&rsquo;ca kerm&ecirc;şan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Wek&icirc; leşker&ecirc;n di şer</p>
<p>Her yek&icirc; b&ucirc; ye nefer</p>
<p>Dikin cenga ker &ucirc; fer</p>
<p>Wey&nbsp; ji derd&ecirc; kerm&ecirc;şan</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp; <strong>ŞERZAN</strong></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>V&ecirc; zilm&ecirc; qeb&ucirc;l nakim</p>
<p>Nizanim ez&ecirc; &ccedil;akim</p>
<p>Bi p&ecirc;n&ucirc;s&ecirc; binv&icirc;sim</p>
<p>Ser&icirc; ber zilm&ecirc; rakim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Lo Şerzano Şerzano</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima em b&ucirc;n erzano</p>
<p>Yek&icirc;t&icirc;ya xwe &ccedil;&ecirc;kin</p>
<p>Bak&ucirc;r baş&ucirc;r xerzano</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rihma Xwed&ecirc; li te be</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av&ecirc; te li r&ecirc; ne be</p>
<p>Şerzan&ecirc; dil&ecirc; me de</p>
<p>Bij&icirc; bi me re hebe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xort&ecirc;n bi x&icirc;ret kuştin</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc;n belengaz h&icirc;ştin</p>
<p>J&icirc;r &ucirc; zana neqandin</p>
<p>Birin m&ecirc;jy&ecirc; wan ş&ucirc;ştin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Razandin me hem&icirc;ya</p>
<p>Beran b&ucirc;n wek&icirc; m&icirc;ya</p>
<p>Bi quret&icirc; fors kirin</p>
<p>Ser ser&ecirc; me Rom&icirc;ya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hewar dikim ji Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bela zaliman bid&ecirc;</p>
<p>Text&ecirc; kujeran hilş&ecirc;</p>
<p>Heyf nem&icirc;ne li erd&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nema rizq &ucirc; av&ecirc; w&icirc;</p>
<p>Li din&ecirc; be nav&ecirc; w&icirc;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; sebr&ucirc; qina&rsquo;et</p>
<p>Bide d&ecirc;y&ucirc; bav&ecirc; w&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em hem&icirc; bibin Şerzan</p>
<p>Herin li pey&icirc; r&ecirc;zan</p>
<p>Wek m&ecirc;ra ser&icirc; bilind</p>
<p>Bisekinin ser p&icirc;yan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Aqil bila li p&ecirc;ş be</p>
<p>Hest &ucirc; h&ecirc;z re serk&ecirc;ş be</p>
<p>Dijmin&ecirc; ,me nikar be</p>
<p>Bila wek&icirc; gam&ecirc;ş be</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Riy&ecirc; dijmin bibe reş</p>
<p>Mekan bi mek&icirc;na xweş</p>
<p>Li ser axeke azad</p>
<p>Roja welat bibe geş</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Id&icirc; bimre neyart&icirc;</p>
<p>Were dinyay&ecirc; aşt&icirc;</p>
<p>Herkes li ser axa xwe</p>
<p>Xweş bij&icirc; bi birat&icirc;.</p>

<h1>USTAD&Ecirc; MIN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ustad&ecirc; min Se&icirc;d N&ucirc;rs&icirc;</p>
<p>Ew rabib&ucirc; li ser kurs&icirc;</p>
<p>He&ccedil;y&ecirc; sual&ecirc; w&icirc; heb&ucirc;n</p>
<p>Dihate cem j&ecirc; dipirs&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bersiva xwe j&ecirc; hildida</p>
<p>Ji rastiy&ecirc; nedb&ucirc; cuda</p>
<p>Bi r&ecirc;berya Ustad&ecirc; min</p>
<p>Ew dikete r&ecirc; ya Xweda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji Nors&ecirc; ji H&icirc;zan&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Girtiy&ecirc; dest&ecirc; Rom&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Dil&ucirc; aql&ecirc; w&icirc; hişyar e</p>
<p>Ne tiral&ecirc; razan&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>B&icirc;st&ucirc; heşt sal ma hepsada</p>
<p>Nexweş b&ucirc; j&icirc;&nbsp; ber xwe dida</p>
<p>Nozdeh cara jehr&icirc; dan&ecirc;</p>
<p>L&ecirc; w&icirc; parastiye Xweda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rab&ucirc; ji aly&ecirc; Bil&icirc;s &ecirc;</p>
<p>Xebatkir heta Tifl&icirc;s &ecirc;</p>
<p>Min pirt&ucirc;k&ecirc;n w&icirc; naskirin</p>
<p>Gava ez di&ccedil;&ucirc;me l&icirc;s&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi bernav Bed&icirc;uzzeman</p>
<p>Xelaskar&ecirc; axirzeman</p>
<p>Alim tev j&ecirc; re tesl&icirc;m b&ucirc;n</p>
<p>Li ber w&icirc; tu zana neman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>W&icirc; gel&ecirc; xwe ji b&icirc;r nekir</p>
<p>Hişyarkir li wan ş&icirc;retkir</p>
<p>Bo xilasya herdu dunya</p>
<p>Cefa kişand pir x&icirc;retkir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Navek&icirc; w&icirc; Mel&ecirc; Menş&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Niv&icirc;sand R&icirc;saley&ecirc;n N&ucirc;r</p>
<p>Tengas&icirc; ji nav me rakir</p>
<p>An&icirc; aram&icirc;y&ucirc; hiz&ucirc;r</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>S&ecirc; meha de w&icirc; xwend&icirc;ye</p>
<p>Tehs&icirc;la xwe qedand&icirc;ye</p>
<p>Seyday&ecirc; w&icirc; li Baz&icirc;d&ecirc;</p>
<p>N&ucirc;r M&ucirc;hemed Celal&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Medresa Zehray&ecirc; dixwest</p>
<p>Bo &ccedil;&ecirc;bibe w&icirc; dikir qest</p>
<p>Temen&ecirc; w&icirc; t&ecirc;r&ecirc; nekir</p>
<p>Ava neb&ucirc; ew neket dest</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zivistan&ecirc; w&icirc; kir hewar</p>
<p>Seva em bib&icirc;nin bihar</p>
<p>Bend&ecirc; zilm&ecirc; ser me rabe</p>
<p>Bi me nikaribe neyar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bavo M&icirc;rze,N&ucirc;r&ecirc; day&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima hewara te nay&ecirc;</p>
<p>Muhemmed Mistefa were</p>
<p>Bav&ecirc; Fatmettuz Zehray&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>YA SITAR</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ziman hilde qontrol&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nakev&icirc; qereqol&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Guhdar bike ker&ecirc; te</p>
<p>Bela nay&ecirc; ser&ecirc; te</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nefs&ecirc; bike wek ker&ecirc;</p>
<p>Swar be here sefer&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&ecirc;l ewtiyan seh neke</p>
<p>Bi wan re tu şer neke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>W&ecirc; bav&ecirc;jin h&ecirc;rsa xwe</p>
<p>Bikevin ser d&ecirc;la xwe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bisekine wek m&ecirc;ran</p>
<p>Derbasbe wek cam&ecirc;ran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Tu xwe bav&ecirc;je Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ew bela wanan bid&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xweda zor e dijwar e</p>
<p>Bi wan tevan dikare</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew d&ecirc;lik&ecirc;n ku dir in</p>
<p>Kopek li pey digerin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bisekine ser p&icirc;yan</p>
<p>Nekeve d&ucirc; hest&icirc;yan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Goşt li ser wan nema ye</p>
<p>Ew para d&ecirc;lika ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>D&ecirc;legur &ucirc;&nbsp; d&ecirc;lese</p>
<p>Bi deng&ecirc; me nehese</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku bibh&icirc;se deng&ecirc; me</p>
<p>Ew&ecirc; here reng&ecirc; me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ka me bi wanan &ccedil;i kir?</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima li me b&ucirc;ne gur?</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew har b&ucirc;ne, b&ucirc;ne dir</p>
<p>Ser me dixin gure gur</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hem&icirc; k&ucirc;&ccedil;ik&ecirc;n hev in</p>
<p>Pey goşt&ecirc; me dikevin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi hev du re direvin</p>
<p>Li ser lepan dikevin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima li me b&ucirc;ne har</p>
<p>Qey&icirc; me para wan xwar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Salek n&icirc;ne vira nin</p>
<p>Kelem&ecirc; &ccedil;av&ecirc; wan in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;avnebar in dexes in</p>
<p>Pir xa&icirc;n in teres in</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dijmin&ecirc; qewm&ecirc; xwe ne</p>
<p>Ew ji cisn&ecirc; kew&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Vediş&ecirc;rin xefikan</p>
<p>Me dixin nav defikan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em ketin tela nefs&ecirc;</p>
<p>Loma em hatin h&ecirc;rs&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gava meriv h&ecirc;rs bibe</p>
<p>Ter &ucirc; hişk tev hev dibe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku meriv dide nav&ecirc;</p>
<p>Nas nake d&ecirc; y&ucirc; bav&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;i t&ecirc; deva dib&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Kela xwe tev dir&ecirc;je</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi zaliman nikare</p>
<p>Ser feq&icirc;ran diqare</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ax hewar hewar hewar</p>
<p>Xweda Rebb&icirc; ya sitar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;i ber&ccedil;avkek ne xweş e</p>
<p>Hem&icirc; reng kirin reş e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nema tu dost nema yar</p>
<p>W&ecirc; hem&icirc; kirin neyar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Feq&icirc;r e, ze&icirc;f e,jar</p>
<p>Dinya li xwe kire bar</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Di bin de zare zar e</p>
<p>Bi v&icirc; bar&icirc; nikare</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bar&ecirc; xwe dayne erd&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xwe bav&ecirc; bext&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew me bisitir&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bin&ecirc; zilm&ecirc; der&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Id&icirc; em nedin nav&ecirc;</p>
<p>Derkevin li ber tav&ecirc;.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>&Ccedil;IMA</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima zarok h&icirc;n nabin</p>
<p>Ser kok&ecirc; h&ecirc;ş&icirc;n nabin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ne exlaq &ucirc; ne edep</p>
<p>Min h&icirc;n nekir &ccedil;i ecep</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nizam hal&ecirc; me &ccedil;abe</p>
<p>A ya me h&ecirc; neb&ucirc; b e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nikarim wek&icirc; jin an</p>
<p>L&ecirc; pir dikim gotin an</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ziman li ser min dir&ecirc;j</p>
<p>Qaşo ez dikim nim&ecirc;j</p>
<p>Qelb&ecirc; min b&ucirc; ye qir&ecirc;j</p>
<p>Ziman&ecirc; min pir dir&ecirc;j</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>K&icirc;jan derd&icirc; bib&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>P&ecirc; kela xwe bav&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kesayeta me nema</p>
<p>Roda bir ava &ccedil;ema</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nizam bi me &ccedil;a b&ucirc; ye</p>
<p>Şerma jin an rab&ucirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Neme pace &ucirc; der&icirc;</p>
<p>Zar pir b&ucirc;ne serser&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; min b&ucirc;ye bir&icirc;n</p>
<p>Herdu &ccedil;av&ecirc;m digir&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gir&icirc;n j&icirc; fayde nake</p>
<p>Pirsgir&ecirc;kan ranake</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi rica ya bi lava</p>
<p>Zar nakin bi ya bav a</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev &ccedil;i rewş e,&ccedil;i hal e?</p>
<p>H&icirc;n neb&ucirc;m s&ecirc;zdeh sal e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mamoste ye nav&ecirc; min</p>
<p>N&icirc;ne s&icirc;h &ucirc; tav&ecirc; min</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dikirim pot&ecirc;n qumaş</p>
<p>Niheq&icirc; dixwim meaş</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dixwim hingiv &ucirc; helew</p>
<p>M&icirc;na ga b&ucirc; me qelew</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev goşta tev heram e</p>
<p>Ji nefs&ecirc; re xulam e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Loma nefis dir b&ucirc; ye</p>
<p>Siq&ecirc;f&ecirc;n w&ecirc; pir b&ucirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rab&ucirc; tofan &ucirc; ba ye</p>
<p>Qewl&ecirc; ley&icirc;n nema ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji kes&icirc; re nab&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>V&ecirc; ji xwe re dib&ecirc;jim.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h1>DERSA BIJ&Icirc;ŞKAN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nojdar&ecirc; me Sedr&ecirc;d&icirc;n</p>
<p>Bibe heyv &ucirc; bedr&ecirc; d&icirc;n</p>
<p>Were dersa R&icirc;sal&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bizanibe qedr&ecirc; d&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bij&icirc;şke &Ucirc;nis Feyat</p>
<p>Yaşam&ecirc; dike xebat</p>
<p>Dib&ecirc; yaşam jiyan e</p>
<p>Xizmeta w&icirc; bo heyat</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ucirc;n&ucirc;s xortek ciwan e</p>
<p>Nojdariy&ecirc; dizane</p>
<p>Nexweşan re pir baş e</p>
<p>Xwe re dike heyran e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Heval&ecirc; wan Enwer e</p>
<p>Dostek&icirc; minewer e</p>
<p>Her hefte ew&ecirc; were</p>
<p>Dizane N&ucirc;r cewher e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ecirc;jaye Kek &ecirc; Neşet</p>
<p>Bi lez e m&icirc;nan&icirc; jet</p>
<p>Gelek kar&ecirc;n x&ecirc;r&ecirc; de</p>
<p>Xebit&icirc; &ucirc; bi ser ket.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xalid min ned&icirc;t&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Nizam bi &ccedil;i reng&icirc; ye</p>
<p>L&ecirc; nav&ecirc; w&icirc; pir xweş e</p>
<p>Ew nav&ecirc; eshab&icirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Doxtorek h&ecirc;ja Haqan</p>
<p>Ocax kir&icirc;ye dikan</p>
<p>Y&ecirc;n ku t&ecirc;ne dikan &ecirc;</p>
<p>Bi xwe re dibin derman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Had&icirc; ye Abdulhad&icirc;</p>
<p>Bi edalet bi dad&icirc;</p>
<p>Qedr&ecirc; n&ucirc;r &ecirc; dizan&icirc;</p>
<p>W&ecirc; bi tu tişt&icirc; nad&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zubey&icirc;r Hebizbin&icirc;</p>
<p>Bejn dir&ecirc;j&icirc; ,ne kin&icirc;</p>
<p>Bo saxkirna nexweşan</p>
<p>Li Batman disekin&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bij&icirc;şk&ecirc; h&ecirc;ja Uzgur</p>
<p>Zora nexweşiy&ecirc; bir</p>
<p>Ji tirs &ucirc; heybeta w&icirc;</p>
<p>M&icirc;qroban mal&ecirc; barkir.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji Farq&icirc;n &ecirc; ye Reş&icirc;t</p>
<p>Zuryeta Adem &ucirc; Ş&icirc;t</p>
<p>Şeytan j&ecirc; vedciniqe</p>
<p>M&icirc;na zinar wek aş&icirc;t</p>
<p>Hec&icirc; Mistefa Ayqal</p>
<p>Him j&ecirc;hat&icirc; him delal</p>
<p>Tu naxwaz&icirc; ez herim</p>
<p>Maf&ecirc; xwe bike helal</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bira y&ecirc; Qasim Acar</p>
<p>Bo n&ucirc;r &ecirc; bibe tucar</p>
<p>Rebb&ecirc; hek&icirc;m &ucirc; Reh&icirc;m</p>
<p>Ew bi we re be her car</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dixtorek&icirc; dilbir&icirc;n</p>
<p>Heye nav&ecirc; w&icirc; Şir&icirc;n</p>
<p>Pispor&ecirc; zarokan e</p>
<p>Ziman &ecirc; w&icirc; şekir&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Were dersa bij&icirc;şkan</p>
<p>Bixwe kade hevr&icirc;şkan</p>
<p>Xweda d&ucirc;r bike derdan</p>
<p>Ne de &ecirc;şa mir&icirc;şkan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Yek b imin re xeberda</p>
<p>Bi cam&ecirc;r&icirc; xwe berda</p>
<p>Got ez te dişbih&icirc;nim</p>
<p>M&icirc;na pis&icirc;ka Seyda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez pis&icirc;ka Seyda bim</p>
<p>Li nava medresa bim</p>
<p>Zikr&ecirc; ya Reh&icirc;m b&ecirc;jim</p>
<p>Guhdariy&ecirc; dersa bim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gel&icirc; bij&icirc;şk,nojdaran</p>
<p>Saxkin nexweş &ucirc; jaran</p>
<p>Ji wan re dev bi ken bin</p>
<p>Eman bidin hewaran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; xwe ji b&icirc;r nekin</p>
<p>Nefs&ecirc; re h&ecirc;s&icirc;r nekin</p>
<p>Şukurdar&ecirc; Xwed&ecirc; bin</p>
<p>X&ecirc;r&ecirc; de qus&ucirc;r nekin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi temen &ucirc; sal&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>Bi meqam &ucirc; mal&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>Bo xwed&ecirc; bi tevger bin</p>
<p>Xweşkin rewş &ucirc; hal&ecirc; xwe</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Pilaqe b&icirc;st &ucirc; yek e</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; bext&ecirc; w&ecirc; veke</p>
<p>Xizmeta N&ucirc;r li Amed</p>
<p>Bix&ecirc;r bike z&ecirc;deke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n bi seyr bi sefer in</p>
<p>H&ucirc;n hem&icirc; bi x&ecirc;r werin</p>
<p>Gulan pir bireş&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Bi silamet vegerin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; me bike ez&icirc;z</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; me bike tem&icirc;z</p>
<p>&Ccedil;i mezin &ccedil;i j&icirc; pi&ccedil;&ucirc;k</p>
<p>&Ccedil;i law dibe &ccedil;i j&icirc; q&icirc;z.</p>

<h1>GUND&Ecirc; BARISL&Ecirc;</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Fat&icirc;h xortek gund&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Hezkiriy&ecirc; Kurd&icirc; ye</p>
<p>Gund&ecirc; wan Barisl&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>Xweş e li ser&ecirc; r&ecirc; ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ku gund&icirc; bibin bira</p>
<p>Nev&ecirc;jin hev kevira</p>
<p>Ku ew wek&icirc; ş&ecirc;ra bin</p>
<p>&Ccedil;i t&ecirc; zur&icirc;na gura</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bidr&ucirc;n berhevkin g&icirc;ya</p>
<p>Bi&ccedil;&ecirc;r&icirc;nin h&ucirc;n m&icirc;ya</p>
<p>Ber xelk&ecirc; st&ucirc;xwar nebin</p>
<p>Bisekinin ser p&icirc;ya</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bes id&icirc; hevdu gez kin</p>
<p>Ji welat&ecirc; xwe hez kin</p>
<p>Zar&ecirc; xwe bidin xwendin</p>
<p>Bo ziman&ecirc; xwe lez kin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Biş&ecirc;r&icirc; nav&ccedil;a me ye</p>
<p>Bostan &ucirc; bax&ccedil;a me ye</p>
<p>Welat hem&icirc; şir&icirc;n e</p>
<p>Dil&ecirc; me par&ccedil;a me ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xelk&ecirc; em paş de h&icirc;ştin</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima me bira kuştin</p>
<p>Tiştek neket dest&ecirc; me</p>
<p>Wek pep&ucirc;kan r&ucirc;niştin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rast&icirc; &ucirc; d&icirc;n &ucirc; &icirc;man</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima bi me re neman</p>
<p>Qenc&icirc; ji nav me derket</p>
<p>&Ccedil;&ucirc; m&icirc;na av&ecirc;n &ccedil;eman</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Fat&icirc;h dib&ecirc;je bes e</p>
<p>Dijmin&ecirc; me teres e</p>
<p>Ew xwe re k&ecirc;f&ecirc; dikin</p>
<p>Para me ten&ecirc; heps e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xay&icirc;nt&icirc; &ucirc; dexes&icirc;</p>
<p>X&ecirc;r j&ecirc; ned&icirc;t tu kes&icirc;</p>
<p>Xirabiyan re b&ecirc;je</p>
<p>Here id&icirc; tu bes&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji nav salan salek&icirc;</p>
<p>Ji M&ucirc;ş &ecirc; hevalek&icirc;</p>
<p>Ev helbesta niv&icirc;sand</p>
<p>Şevek bi silavek&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Min ew&icirc; nas nedikir</p>
<p>Ew&icirc; pere h&ucirc;r dikir</p>
<p>Şeva Rexa&icirc;b&ecirc; b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Ev helbest min re &ccedil;&ecirc;kir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav&icirc; w&icirc; j&icirc; Ra&icirc;f e</p>
<p>Ne Ar&icirc;f &ucirc; Na&icirc;f e</p>
<p>Xwed&ecirc; bike para me</p>
<p>Peqlewe ,qeda&icirc;f e.</p>

<h1>XWEDAWO ! ME! BERAET KE !</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Li Sas&ucirc;n gund&ecirc; Bil&icirc;s im</p>
<p>Ev&ecirc; helbest&ecirc; dinv&icirc;sim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em hatin li vir taz&icirc;y&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ez dinv&icirc;sim v&ecirc; yaz&icirc;y&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rihmet l&ecirc; be k&icirc; mir&icirc;ye</p>
<p>Ji dinya y&ecirc; ko&ccedil; kir&icirc;ye</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;van&ecirc; mele Yilmaz im</p>
<p>Şikir &icirc;şev bi n&icirc;yaz im</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Yilmaz bi r&ecirc;z bi hurmet e</p>
<p>&Icirc;şev şeva beraet e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hozan im bi şeref şan im</p>
<p>Ji gunehan ez poşman im</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew qus&ucirc;r&ecirc;n ku bor&icirc; ne</p>
<p>Xweda li me bibor&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me ji xwe re bike n&ecirc;z e</p>
<p>Ji gunehan bipar&ecirc;ze</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>X&ucirc;y &ucirc; exlaq&ecirc; me baş ke</p>
<p>Ew xeberdana me xweş ke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Me bipar&ecirc;ze ji le&rsquo;&icirc;n</p>
<p>Bide me da qewl&ecirc; ley&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zarok&ecirc;n me bibin xilas</p>
<p>Şukurdar bin bikin sipas</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo naskirin&ecirc; lez bikin</p>
<p>Ji Rebb&ecirc; xwe pir hez bikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Biterk&icirc;nin tiraliyan</p>
<p>Id&icirc; nekin xirabiyan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bi taet bin nim&ecirc;j bikin</p>
<p>Şeytan &ucirc; nefs&ecirc; g&ecirc;j bikin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bixw&icirc;nin dersa Quran&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xilas bikin em &icirc;man&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bar&ecirc; p&icirc;roz hildin pişt&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bibin lay&icirc;q&ecirc; buh&icirc;şt&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Sas&ucirc;n &ucirc; Tat&icirc;k &ucirc; V&ecirc;rvan</p>
<p>Nem&icirc;nin b&ecirc; nan &ucirc; arvan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nan&ecirc; tend&ucirc;r&ecirc; nebe k&ucirc;t</p>
<p>T&ecirc;r bixwe Axpirak &ucirc; Kut</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Birabin Kelhok Mişk&icirc;n&ucirc;s</p>
<p>Nexeydin L&icirc; &ucirc; Darin&ucirc;s</p>

<p>Bidin li pey bav &ucirc; day&ecirc;</p>
<p>Herin N&ucirc;rs&ecirc; &ucirc; Xeyda y&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ronya &Ccedil;evan şefaet ke</p>
<p>Rebb&ecirc; xef&ucirc;r beraet ke</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Em bixw&icirc;nin nebin nezan</p>
<p>Ji xelkan re bibin r&ecirc;zan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>N&icirc;şan bidin em r&ecirc; &ucirc; p&ecirc;</p>
<p>Bila gel rast li pey me b&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nekevin nava şaşiyan</p>
<p>Bikin qenc&icirc; &ucirc; başiyan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hey neviy&ecirc;n Ş&ecirc;x Şabed&icirc;n</p>
<p>Sey&icirc;d El&icirc;,Mihme Şir&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Tucar nebin evd&ecirc;n evda</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>Bibin ron&icirc; v&ecirc;xin &ccedil;iran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bibin ş&ecirc;x &ucirc; sertac&ecirc;n me</p>
<p>Ji derdan re &icirc;lac&ecirc;n me</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Rakin dur&ucirc;t&icirc;,n&icirc;faq &ecirc;</p>
<p>B&icirc;nin aşt&icirc; &ucirc; w&icirc;faq &ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Evan xelkan li hev b&icirc;nin</p>
<p>Dest&ecirc;n wan bi hev bix&icirc;nin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ereb ,Faris,Tirk &ucirc; Kurdan</p>
<p>Xweda xilas ke ji derdan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>AX ! ZEHRA AX !</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&Ccedil;ima ez neb&ecirc;jim ax</p>
<p>Bo &ccedil;i neb&ecirc;jim hey wax</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ya hezkir&icirc; Zehra b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Gula Ronya &Ccedil;eva b&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ke&ccedil;ika Xed&icirc;c&ecirc; b&ucirc;</p>
<p>Dayika Zeyneb&ecirc; b&ucirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Diya Hesen Husey&icirc;n</p>
<p>P&icirc;rka Zeynel Abid&icirc;n</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dayik&ecirc; ew z&ucirc; berda</p>
<p>Ma di nava nemerda</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>M&ecirc;r&ecirc;n heval&ecirc;n El&icirc;</p>
<p>Qel&icirc;yan b&ucirc;ne xwel&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xa&icirc;n li nav Kerbela</p>
<p>Li Huseyn b&ucirc;ne bela</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ecirc;n ku soz da ew xapand</p>
<p>Ten&ecirc; ber bi &ccedil;ol&ecirc; şand</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xistine nav agiran</p>
<p>H&icirc;ştin li nava guran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Fatimay&ecirc; l&ecirc; day&ecirc;</p>
<p>Wey reben&ecirc; Zehra y&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Deng&ecirc; berx&ecirc; te nay&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ma li nav Kerbela y&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Huseyn ten&ecirc; ye jar e</p>
<p>Yez&icirc;d gurek&icirc; har e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>T&ecirc; deng&ecirc; z&ucirc;re z&ucirc;ran</p>
<p>Civyane koma guran</p>

<p>&Ccedil;iqas zar&ecirc; w&ecirc; hene</p>

<p>Bi rik in bi ş&icirc;qaqin</p>
<p>Gotina hevdu nakin</p>

<p>Hene bi sed an deh an</p>
<p>Hev nab&icirc;nin bi meh an</p>

<p>Li hev nakin silav&ecirc;</p>

<p>Pirt&ucirc;k t&ecirc;n wan ranakin</p>
<p>Der&ecirc; wana venakin</p>

<h1>POSTEVAN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Postevan postevan e</p>
<p>R&icirc;sale li mila ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Postevan postevan e</p>
<p>N&ucirc;bihar li mila ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bar&ecirc; li mil giran e</p>
<p>Biha ye ne erzan e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;B&ecirc; bazbend b&ecirc; nivişt e</p>
<p>T&ucirc;rik&ecirc; N&ucirc;r li pişt e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew b&ecirc; bask e b&ecirc; per e</p>
<p>Gelek c&icirc;yan digere</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kar&ecirc; dike p&icirc;roz e</p>
<p>Riza Heq j&ecirc; re doz e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bimbarek bi &icirc;xlas e</p>
<p>Ev peyw&icirc;r j&ecirc; re xas e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Serposte Ebdurrehman</p>
<p>Siwar&ecirc; hesp&ecirc; rehwan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ji bajar&ecirc; Batman&ecirc;</p>
<p>Heta bigre c&icirc;han&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ron&icirc;y&ecirc; diweş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Gav bi gav direş&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Van derman &ucirc; &icirc;lacan</p>
<p>Dig&icirc;h&icirc;ne muhtacan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Derd dib&icirc;nin deway&ecirc;</p>
<p>&Ecirc;ş dib&icirc;nin ş&icirc;fay&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ew difroşe cewheran</p>
<p>Nay&ecirc; p&icirc;van bi peran</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Gewher almaste dur e</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; bi aqil dikire</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dikire dipar&ecirc;ze</p>
<p>J&ecirc; re digire r&ecirc;z e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Cewher ji Quran&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>Şemal&ecirc;n &icirc;man&ecirc; ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Nav R&icirc;saley&ecirc;n N&ucirc;r e</p>
<p>Ev dem manew&icirc; ş&ucirc;r e</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo dewra helaket&ecirc;</p>
<p>Ew dike v&ecirc; xebat&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo xilaske &icirc;nsanan</p>
<p>Ji xeter &ucirc; xusranan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dil da guman nem&icirc;ne</p>
<p>Bawer&icirc; pak bim&icirc;ne</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ev n&ucirc;r bibe elamet</p>
<p>&Icirc;man bibe silamet</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dexil here b&ecirc;der&ecirc;</p>
<p>Hilas be li mehşer&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Aq&icirc;beta me x&ecirc;r be</p>
<p>&Ccedil;av &ucirc; dil&ecirc; me t&ecirc;r be</p>

<p>Neb&icirc;nin em xelay&ecirc;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Bo em bikin xizmet&ecirc;</p>
<p>Xweda bide taqet&ecirc;.</p>

<h1>PAŞGOTIN</h1>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez bi x&ecirc;ra N&ucirc;bihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>Şikir derketim bihar&ecirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kek &lsquo;El&icirc;, Kek&ecirc; Suleyman</p>
<p>Du heb fedakar&ecirc; Kurdan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Sabah hat dibistan vekir</p>
<p>Wan xwendekar l&ecirc; z&ecirc;de kir</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Dibistan b&ucirc; panzde sal&icirc;</p>
<p>Kurd hem&icirc; hatine al&icirc;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Xebat kirin wan mil bi mil</p>
<p>Dest hev girtin bi can &ucirc; dil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ez v&ecirc; li xwe mikur t&icirc;nim</p>
<p>Ez bi saya wan dixw&icirc;nim</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Hezar nehsid nod&ucirc; dudu</p>
<p>Gul &ucirc; Bilbil gih&icirc;şt hevdu</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kurd b&ucirc;n bilbil, ziman b&ucirc; gul</p>
<p>B&ecirc;na xweş hat kete b&ecirc;fil</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Y&ecirc; ku helbest y&ecirc; ku niv&icirc;s</p>
<p>Xistne t&ucirc;rik xistne tel&icirc;s</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Heta dev t&ucirc;r tij&icirc; b&ucirc; mişt</p>
<p>Ke&ccedil; &ucirc; xortan hildane pişt</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>X&ecirc;ra kala &ccedil;ira v&ecirc;ket</p>
<p>Karwan&ecirc; me Kurdan r&ecirc;ket</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Mezin &ucirc; r&ecirc;zan li p&ecirc;ş in</p>
<p>J&rsquo;me ra ş&icirc;retan dib&ecirc;jin</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Zarok &ucirc; ke&ccedil;, xort &ucirc; ciwan</p>
<p>Em tev bajon, herin d&ucirc; wan</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Yek&ucirc;, dudu, sis&ecirc; &ucirc; &ccedil;ar</p>
<p>Ji &ccedil;anda xwe nebin b&ecirc; par</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Herkes t&ecirc;ra taqeta xwe</p>
<p>Berdewam ke xebata xwe.</p>
